Italian-Abyssinian Dispute 83

Abyssinian Government Asks League of Nations to Handle

(Geneva) The Geneva League of Nations Secretariat received a telegram from the Abyssinian government, requesting the League of Nations Secretariat to convene a meeting of the Executive Council to consider the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia. The telegram stated that Italian troops are now gathered in the Zhelogubi area and attacked the Abyssinian defense forces there on December 28, killing two people and wounding two others. Italian planes are soaring in the area, and tanks are also maneuvering nearby. Therefore, the Abyssinian government, in accordance with Article 11 of the League of Nations Covenant, requests that measures be taken to safeguard peace immediately. After receiving this telegram, Geneva felt like a bolt from the blue. League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol has telegraphed back, stating that he is currently distributing the document to the members of the Executive Council and will convene a meeting on January 11. People in Geneva believe that Abyssinia's request may cause more disputes in the Franco-Italian negotiations in Rome, because one of the topics to be negotiated between France and Italy is the interests of France and Italy in Somalia and Abyssinia in Africa. After the Italian government received the Abyssinian government's document in Geneva, it immediately stated that the Italian army had not engaged in any aggression or bombing and that the Italian army had been stationed in Afdubai for several years. Because Abyssinia had military operations in the disputed area, it had to send planes to reconnaissance. (Reuters Telegram, 4th)

(Geneva) The Italian government has responded to the most recent document from the Abyssinian government to the League of Nations, stating: (1) Italian troops have not advanced into Abyssinian territory; (2) The Afdubai area referred to by the Abyssinian government belongs to the Wal-Wal area, and the Wal-Wal area is indeed guarded by Italian troops; (2) Italian troops did not bomb the Gerlogubi area; (4) Italian aircraft reconnaissance was necessary because a large number of Abyssinian troops were concentrated near Wal-Wal and the Wal-Wal area. It was signed by Italian Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs Suvich. After this reply was issued, the Abyssinian government then telegraphed the League of Nations, requesting that the dispute be handled in accordance with Article 11 of the Covenant. (Havas Telegram, 3rd)

Saar Plebiscite Approaching 84

German Front Prepares for Demonstration

Saarbrücken. The Saar plebiscite is imminent, and organized communist and separatist factions have begun to engage in intense activities, using terrorist methods to disrupt local security. Numerous riots have occurred in recent days. (National Telegram, 2nd)

Saarbrücken. Yesterday, the German Front Group and the Anti-National Socialist Party United Front Group held grand election rallies separately. The process was orderly, and no incidents occurred. The German Front Group is scheduled to march in a demonstration on Sunday and advance here. According to the Labor News, the group has already booked 48 special trains for its members to ride in. (Havas Telegram, 4th)

Cash Inflow to US Reaches 400 Million Yuan 85

Silver Purchase Law Completely Ineffective

(Washington) It was announced here today that since June of last year, the cash inflow to the United States has reached a huge sum of 400 million US dollars. Therefore, the government's attempt to increase the silver reserves in the national treasury to one-third of the gold reserves in accordance with the regulations of the 1934 silver purchase has become completely ineffective as a result. Although the Ministry of Finance has purchased a large amount of silver in the world silver market, according to the Associated Press statistics, it is still far from the goal of purchasing silver. On May 31 last year, the total value of gold was $7,778,883,214, and the total value of silver was $832,762,767, which was only 10.7% of the gold reserves. By December 29, the number of gold reserves had increased to $8,232,732,078, while the number of silver reserves was still only $1,027,464,169, which was only 13.2% of the gold reserves. Therefore, after half a year of government silver purchases, the only result was to increase the silver reserve ratio by 2.5%. If the original goal is to be achieved, experts calculate that another 133 million ounces of silver must be purchased. At the same time, the Associated Press also learned that only 200 million yuan of the United States' 200 billion yuan balance fund has been used, and its use is not limited to one item.

(National Telegram, 3rd)

Change of Governor of the Bank of France 86

Policy of Maintaining the Gold Standard Remains Unchanged

(Paris) It was announced here today that Tannery has replaced Moret as Governor of the Bank of France. The reason for the change has not been explained. However, Tannery is a proponent of the public sale of treasury bonds, which is the same opinion as French Prime Minister Flandin and contrary to Moret's opinion. Finance Minister Germain, Benard, and Tannery's appointment as Governor of the Bank of France said that the current policies of the Ministry of Finance will not change. The plan of former President Poincaré to revive national finances will continue to be carried out, and Moret's advocacy of maintaining the franc will also be maintained. He and the new governor are determined to support the gold standard. It was previously rumored in French financial circles that the government planned to issue treasury bonds totaling 200 billion francs for private purchase, but they could be discounted and purchased by the Bank of France. Moret did not agree with this policy. Now that Tannery has been appointed as governor, it proves that the previous saying had a basis. It is said that this policy of the government is the result of a large increase in the issuance of banknotes, but the subsequent reduction in interest rates should offset the impact of rising prices. Because it is difficult to raise long-term loans, the government will have no way to cope with the debts of 1935 unless it adopts this new policy. Some say that the French government wants to imitate the British cheap currency policy so that it can drop back to long-term loans in the future. The announcement of Tannery's appointment as Governor of the Bank of France and the news that France and Italy have reached an agreement have caused a boom in the exchange. French public bonds rose 135 centimes, and other bonds also rose one after another. (Reuters Telegram, 2nd)

Anglo-Irish Agreement Established 87

Free State Livestock Traded for British Coal

(London) The Irish Free State and the British government have signed a gentleman's agreement, which stipulates that the Irish Free State will purchase a certain number of tons of British coal, and the United Kingdom will allow the import of livestock of equal value from Ireland. Many view this agreement as an important step towards restoring normal relations between Britain and Ireland, and some hope that this development may lead to progress in the existing political problems between Britain and Ireland. As a result of this agreement, British coal imports to the Irish Free State will increase by more than one million tons, and Irish livestock imports to the United Kingdom will increase by 150,000 heads. (Reuters Telegram, 2nd)

(London) According to Dominion Minister Thomas, it is expected that the Irish Free State will purchase all of its coal from Britain in the future. British coal exports to the Irish Free State can be expected to increase by approximately 1.25 million tons annually, and British coal mines will increase recruitment by 5,000 workers as a result. According to Irish Free State leader de Valera today, this Anglo-Irish agreement is one of the Free State government's constant expressions of willingness to make understanding. If there are opportunities to continue to make the same understanding as today in the future, it is expected that both sides will accept them in the same spirit. (Reuters Telegram, 3rd)

Lin Bai Zi Kidnapping Case Trial Opens 88

Lin Bai Couple Appear in Court to Testify

Flemington – Hauptmann, the German carpenter and principal offender in the Lin Bai Zi kidnapping case, was brought to trial at the court here today. The young lawyer Wilentz first stated the charges, saying, "We will prove that the perpetrator of this crime sits before the court today." As he spoke, he pointed to the defendant. He then described in detail the circumstances of the crime, stating that the defendant used a ladder to sneak into Lin Bai's son's bedroom, carried him out of bed, and inadvertently broke the ladder while descending, causing the child to fall to his death. The defendant then took the child's pajamas to negotiate the ransom. Wilentz then described the situation of identifying the body at the graveyard. The jurors looked sorrowful upon hearing this. After Wilentz finished his speech, the defendant's lawyer Reilly requested that the trial be invalidated because Wilentz was trying to move the jurors with tragic words, which was detrimental to the defendant. However, this motion was rejected by the judge. Mrs. Lin Bai testified in court, speaking in a low voice with tears in her eyes, describing in detail the window through which her son was stolen, and accurately identifying her son's toys, film and sleeveless vest, saying that she had personally made them. Mrs. Lin stood in the witness stand for forty-five minutes. The defendant Hauptmann initially sat blankly, staring at the people in front of him, but when Mrs. Lin Bai gave her testimony, he showed signs of unease. Colonel Lin Bai then testified that on the night his son was stolen, he opened the door and heard the sound of a ladder falling. (Reuters dispatch from the 3rd)

Flemington – Reilly, the lawyer defending Hauptmann, announced today that he intends to broadcast his defense, stating that he will prove that this case was a conspiracy within the Lin Bai's house, but none of the Lin Bai family was involved. There were five accomplices in total, whose names will be announced in court. The child was apparently carried directly out of the upstairs, rather than stolen from the nurse's window using a ladder. It is reported that Reilly has been practicing law for 25 years and has handled over a thousand murder cases. (Reuters dispatch from the 4th)

Citroën Company Partially Resumes Production 89

(Paris) – Citroën, which had requested bankruptcy liquidation at the end of last year due to the impact of the economic panic, resumed production in part today with the assistance of the government. Three thousand workers have already started working, and another batch will be recruited next Monday. This morning, a large number of workers gathered in front of the factory, hoping to resume work, and the order was good, without any incidents. (Havas dispatch from the 3rd)

The time for the Saar vote is near (French Communications)

The focus of the Franco-German dispute

The coal and iron relationship is most important

If France and Italy unite, Germany will become even more isolated 90

The Saar region, with an area of only 190,000 square kilometers and a population of only 780,000, occupies such an important position between France and Germany that it could even cause changes throughout Europe. In the past, when the Paris Peace Conference was held, this land caused opposition from British Prime Minister Lloyd George and American President Wilson. As a result, it was agreed that a general vote of the local people would be held on January 13, 1935, to determine whether the Saar should belong to Germany or France.

In terms of local ethnic relations, more than 90 percent of the people are of German descent. They all speak German and have the customs of Germany. The French account for only 3 to 5 percent. Therefore, in the fifteen years since the end of the war until recently, France has spent tens of millions of francs each year to establish French elementary schools and technical schools there, but the results have not been very good, and the number of students has decreased year by year. Other efforts to buy people's hearts, such as news media and cultural lectures, have not been able to achieve the expected results.

Originally, Germany ruled the Saar before the Treaty of Versailles, for more than a century from 1816 to 1918, while France held the area for only 22 years from 1792 to 1815. Therefore, the German people account for the vast majority of the local population. It is naturally impossible to change the people's thinking in a short period of one or two decades, when European nationalism is still prevalent. If we speculate according to common sense, the results of the vote may not be favorable to France. If the current Germany does not oppress Jews or Catholics, then the Saar people will certainly vote to return to Germany. At present, the people living in the Saar are concerned about their own safety and feel the future political oppression, so they cannot help but hesitate about the issue of returning to Germany.

In fact, France prepared for this move when it signed the Treaty of Versailles, separating the ground security and the underground minerals. The treaty stipulates that if the Saar region votes to return to Germany, then Germany must prepare cash to buy the minerals, otherwise the Saar's coal and iron mines will still belong to France.

In 1933, the Saar's monthly average production was 130,000 tons of pig iron, 140,000 tons of steel, and 880,000 tons of coal. Its pig iron production is approximately 29 percent of the total production of Germany and 24 percent of the total production of France. Steel production is approximately 22 percent of the total production of Germany and 24 percent of France. This shows its important position. Germany naturally wants to use this to restore its national power, and France also wants to use it to stabilize its hegemony. In particular, after Germany advocated the abolition of the Treaty of Versailles, Britain also hinted at sympathy, and Italy clearly stated that the treaty should be revised immediately. Therefore, the former French Foreign Minister Barthou traveled extensively, first communicating fully with the small countries surrounding Germany's borders, such as the Danube River basin countries, and unanimously supporting the Treaty of Versailles and the League of Nations. Fearing that their strength was weak and insufficient to subdue Germany, he also brought the Soviet Union into the League of Nations, vaguely forming an alliance. As a result, the foundation of the League of Nations in Europe was further consolidated, and Britain naturally had to express its alignment with the League of Nations. The only remaining problem was the relationship with Italy. If Barthou had not been assassinated in Marseille, he would have visited the Blackshirt Prime Minister to discuss this issue after sending back the King of Yugoslavia. Now Laval has succeeded him and is still paying close attention to the work of uniting with Italy.

Since the European continental countries are all focused on maintaining the status quo, Germany is inevitably diplomatically isolated. Even if Germany wins the vote on January 13, it will only gain political control on the ground. To take control of the minerals, it must still use cash to buy them. Otherwise, it will only be possible to forcibly break the Treaty of Versailles. However, in diplomacy, except for Poland's slightly better feelings towards Germany, the remaining countries cannot be considered allies. Moreover, France still has the right to send troops into the Saar according to the treaty, and is already preparing. Germany's strength, whether in military or economic terms, is insufficient to cope with war, and it cannot use the League of Nations. The best outcome is probably still for the League of Nations to continue to manage it. (December 1st, Paris)

Detailed Account of Zhang Weicun's Death in Shandong 91

Shot dead on the spot at the Jinde Association

His follower Yang Jinjian was also injured in the neck at the same time

The murderer is on the run, only dozens of suspects have been apprehended

Han reports to the Central Government and orders the military and police to arrest the murderer

Jinan correspondence, Zhang Weicun, alternate member of the Central Executive Committee, concurrently standing committee member of the Shandong Provincial Party Department and member of the Provincial Government, was suddenly attacked tonight (2nd) at the Jinde Association after guiding the New Life Movement lantern parade. He was shot five times and died on the spot. His follower Yang Jinjian was also injured in the neck and was admitted to the hospital for treatment. All three murderers escaped without a trace. After the incident, dozens of suspects were apprehended while searching the visitors and are currently being interrogated. It is generally speculated that Zhang's tragic death was mostly due to an assassination by reactionary elements. The details are as follows:

Today (2nd) was the second day of the Shandong New Life Movement lantern parade. It was stipulated in advance that Zhang Weicun of the Provincial Party Committee was responsible for guiding it. The assembly point was in the Huangting Stadium in the city, and the time was 6:00 PM. Zhang had dinner at his private residence on Xiemalu at 4:00 PM and went to the Provincial Party Department in the city at 5:00 PM to inspect and urge the Party Department personnel to go to the assembly quickly. At 6:00 PM, he went to the Huangting Stadium to speak to the people participating in the lantern parade, and said that he would go to the Jinde Association and agreed to meet everyone at the Jinde Association. Then he went to the Jinde Association in the commercial port with Provincial Government Advisor Ma Qianli and Councilor Zhao Yunxie in a car. After entering the association, Ma and Zhao went to the Jingju Theater to watch a play. Zhang wanted to find a place for the people of the lantern parade, so he took his follower Yang Jinjian and walked along the front of the association's office from north to south. The place was relatively remote, so there were very few visitors. Unexpectedly, when they walked to the west of the Peacock Pavilion behind the banquet hall, at about 6:50 PM, there were three people ambushing there. One tall person was wearing a gray cotton robe, and the other two were shorter than the person in gray. They took out their guns and first shot at Zhang's follower Yang Jinjian. Yang was injured and fell to the ground. The murderers continued to fire many shots at Zhang, who was shot five times and died on the spot. Zhang and Yang both carried guns, but because the incident happened suddenly, they did not have time to open fire. After committing the crime, the murderers dispersed and fled. When the military and police in the association heard the sound and rushed to the scene, the murderers had already disappeared. They saw Zhang lying in a pool of blood with his head facing south and his feet facing north. His follower Yang Jinjian was also next to him. Because Yang was shot in the neck and did not injure the esophagus, his life was not in danger. He was immediately carried to Jinan Hospital for treatment, while Zhang's flesh

Page 15

was blurred, his brain was outside, blood was flowing all over the ground, and he died without hope of recovery.

After the incident, Li Shuchun, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Wang Shiqi, Director of the Public Security Bureau, Shi Jingzhou, Director of the Military Law Department, and Wu Huawen, Commander of the Garrison, all rushed to the scene after hearing the news. They immediately ordered the military and police to impose a temporary curfew, banning pedestrians from passing by the Jinde Association and searching the association separately. Three bullet casings were found at the scene of the incident, which could be identified as having been used by a Browning pistol, but no murder weapon was found. At that time, the Jingju Garden and Dagu Book Field in the Jinde Association were all performing, so they temporarily sent people to guard the door, prohibiting people from leaving. On the one hand, they checked the visitors at the gate, first letting the women and children in the garden out, and then letting the visitors in each garden out in batches, all of whom were searched by the military and police one by one. Those whose appearance was suspicious, except for legitimate merchants who were allowed to leave, were closed in a separate room for questioning. By midnight, all the visitors had left, and Li Shuchun and others questioned the dozens of suspects separately and then handed them over to the enforcement team and the Public Security Bureau for detention.

When Zhang Weicun was shot, his wife, Ms. Liu Jinwen, was watching a play in the Jingju Theater, and she did not expect that her husband would suddenly suffer a tragic death. After returning home, she heard the news and immediately rushed back to the Jinde Association. Seeing her husband die tragically, she cried bitterly. Before long, Zhang Shengxi, supervisor of the Provincial Party Department (Zhang Weicun's uncle), Li Ziqian, executive member, and others also rushed to the scene. They immediately found someone to carry Zhang's body back to the Zhang residence at No. 6 Xiaowei Road, Jingliu Road, preparing to put it in a coffin tomorrow (3rd). At 10:00 PM that night, the Zhang residence first invited a doctor to the residence to wash the wounds on Zhang's body. Before long, Zhou Wenbin, the chief prosecutor of the local court, personally went to the Zhang residence to examine the body. It was counted that Zhang had suffered five injuries. One bullet entered the right cheek and exited the left cheek. One bullet entered the temple and exited the left temple. Two other bullets passed through the sides of the lower abdomen and penetrated out of the back. One bullet passed through the left arm, only injuring the outer skin.

Zhang Weicun was from Shandong. In addition to handling Party affairs, he was also engaged in social undertakings such as schools, hospitals, and charities. Therefore, the members of the Provincial Party Department and people from all walks of life went to offer condolences that night. After hearing about Wei Cun's death, Han Fuju, Chairman of the Provincial Government, was very saddened. In addition to sending a telegram to the Central Party Department and Chairman Jiang and President Wang to report and request a posthumous award for Zhang, he also ordered the military and police to strictly arrest the murderer and bring them to justice. Zhang was thirty-eight years old this year. He still has a grandfather named Wenbin, who is eighty-five years old this year. Zhang's father, Jingting, is fifty-nine years old this year, and his mother, Leng, is sixty-two years old. He has one younger brother, named Fuju, who is fourteen years old, and a son named Minsheng, who is also fourteen years old, studying at Donglu Middle School in this city. Zhang's wife, Ms. Liu Jinwen, is thirty-five years old this year. (Night of the 2nd)

Another report, since the assassination of Liu Lianyi, a member of the Provincial Party Department, in Shandong Province in the nineteenth year, there have been very few similar incidents involving Party and government workers. Unexpectedly, at 7:00 PM last night (2nd), Zhang Weicun, an alternate member of the Central Executive Committee, standing committee member of the Shandong Provincial Party Department, and member of the Provincial Government, was suddenly assassinated and died. Today (3rd), the military and police agencies are cooperating to arrest the murderer and have offered a reward of 50,000 yuan for the arrest of the murderer. There is still no news. No murder weapon was found in the Jinde Association, the scene of the incident. It is generally suspected that the murderer is a well-organized group. The body has been placed in a coffin tonight (3rd) and the aftermath is being handled. Key figures from the Party, government, and military are all going to offer condolences. The following is a further record of the news from all sides:

Relatives Expressed: Chairman Han paid close attention to the assassins' guns and ordered a thorough search to capture them for research, but so far, nothing has been found. According to Zhang Zhuxi, Zhang's uncle and supervisor of the Provincial Party Department, there are no clues in this case at present. It is impossible to make a hasty judgment on what kind of person committed the crime, but judging from the circumstances at the time of the incident, it does not seem to be a private feud, because a private feud would only involve one person who held a grudge. Now there are at least three murderers, who were calm and composed, which is obviously an organized action. Four of the shots fired hit the head, and their accurate, skilled technique also shows that they are accustomed to this, which cannot be compared to those who vent their anger rashly. However, the three murderers had at least three guns. After the incident, it is estimated that they must have abandoned their guns and tried to escape. On the one hand, the gate was guarded and inspected, but as a result, from last night until now, the ditches, toilets, and garbage piles in the garden have been searched almost everywhere, but no trace has been found. It is really incomprehensible where the assassins came from.

Reward for Arresting the Murderer: After this incident occurred, Han Fuju, Chairman of the Provincial Government, sent a telegram to the Central Party Department, the Executive Yuan, and other places to report, and at the same time strictly arrested the murderer. Jinan is the location of the provincial capital, with tight defenses, and the Jinde Association is even more densely populated by military and police. The murderer openly killed the Party and government officials, which is extremely bold. He ordered the arrest to be brought to justice, and issued a notice offering a reward for the arrest of the murderer. The text reads: (Zhang Weicun, a member of the Shandong Provincial Party Department, was attacked by bandits at the Jinde Association. Those who can report inside information to solve the case will be given a reward of 20,000 yuan. Those who can fully disclose the case and solve it will be given a reward of 50,000 yuan. The funds are deposited and will not be broken. Shandong Provincial Government, January 3rd,)

Handling the Aftermath: After Zhang Weicun's death, the aftermath is being handled. This morning (3rd), Chairman Han convened a meeting of the directors, members, Chief of Staff Liu Shuxiang, Director of the Military Law Department Shi Jingzhou, Jinan Garrison Commander Wu Huawen, and Director of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau Wang Shiqi in the Provincial Government to discuss the aftermath and offer a reward for the arrest of the murderer. At 8:00 AM, Wei Cun's wife, Liu Jinwen, in plain clothes, went to the Provincial Government to see Han, prostrated herself on the ground and cried for the arrest of the murderer. Han told her about the reward and the strict orders for the arrest, and told her that the public would take full responsibility for the affairs after the death of Committee Member Zhang, and asked her to rest assured. Liu thanked him with tears and left. The funeral preparation office has been established, with three directors: Li Tianni, Councilor of the Provincial Government, Cao Junfeng, Deputy Director of the Reception Office, and Li Wenzhai, Standing Committee Member of the Provincial Party Department. Zhang's remains have been placed in a coffin today (3rd). The coffin is made of cypress wood and is worth more than 400 yuan. Zhang's residence has been set up with sheds to prepare for the funeral at a fixed time. Han Fuju (Han also serves as the Standing Committee of the Provincial Party Department) notified the Provincial Party Department today that after the death of Committee Member Zhang, the staff of the Standing Committee will continue to work as usual and cannot be changed. No meetings may be held without his consent. The Provincial Party Department has decided to close the office for one day tomorrow (4th), and all staff will go to pay their respects.

Suspects: After the incident last night (2nd), the Jinde Association was temporarily under curfew and the visitors were checked. The old, weak, women and children were released, and those who were slightly suspicious were detained. There are currently 52 people detained in the Public Security Bureau, 13 people in the General Headquarters Military Law Department, and the number of people in the Garrison Command is unknown. They are being interrogated separately today (3rd). The following is a record of the confessions of the 13 people in the Military Law Department:

Lin Ruiting: Confessed that he is 25 years old, from Qixia County, and graduated from the Higher Police Academy. He is currently interning at the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau. At about 6:00 PM last night, he went to Jinde with Mou Mengji to watch a play. He did not know about the shooting and did not know Committee Member Zhang. The confession is true.

Xu Dexuan: Confessed that he is 37 years old, from Qianxu Village, west of Huang County. He used to write at the Huang County Party Department, but because there were too many people, he went to write at the Third Section of the County Government. Because he came to Jinan to pay a fine, he was listening to a play at the Jinde Association at 6:00 PM last night. He never left the theater and was arrested. He did not hear the shooting, and knew nothing about Committee Member Zhang. The confession is true.

Wang Jiakang: Confessed that he is 19 years old, from Licheng County, and lives at No. 55 Shuanglong Street, Dongguan. He was an apprentice at the Fengyu Gong Electric Appliance Store in the commercial port last year. Because the business closed, he is now delivering newspapers for Shandong Minbao. Last night, he heard a shooting at the Jinde Association. He initially thought it was firecrackers, but later heard that it was a shooting. At that time, he wanted to go out, but the gatekeeper would not let him go, so he turned back to find his companion. He was arrested near the root of the large bird cage. He does not know who assassinated Committee Member Zhang. The confession is true.

Zhang Xinwu: Confessed that he is 25 years old, from Wudi County, and lives on Nanmen Street in the city. He is an assistant at the Licheng County Party Department. He was introduced by Zhao Shilian. At 7:00 PM last night, he was watching a play at the Jinde Association. When he was about to come out, the gatekeeper asked him what he was doing. He said he was an assistant at the County Party Department and was not allowed to leave. He did not know why at that time. He did not hear the shooting of Committee Member Zhang at the Jinde Association. He does not know who assassinated him. The confession is true.

Zhao Jingyu: Confessed that he is 20 years old, from Licheng County, and lives at No. 5 Yongsheng Street, Nanguan. He is currently an apprentice at the Yuanshun Used Clothing Store in the New Market. At 6:30 PM last night, he was watching a play at the Jinde Association. He picked up a package of tickets on the floor of the opera theater and hid them in his arms. He did not know they were military tickets. He did not know the number of tickets until he was caught. He was watching a play when the shooting happened and knew nothing about it. The confession is true.

Liu Jiagan: Confessed that he is 30 years old, from Cheng County, and lives in Fuyong Village, Fourth District, northwest of the city. He used to be a clerk at the Yangxin County Party Department, but he quit in June last year. In September this year, he came out of his home and lived at No. 51 Linqixiang South Street, at his sister's husband Lu Bingan's place. His sister's husband is a clerk at the Provincial Party Department, and his second sister and brother are all clerks at the Provincial Party Department. He and Committee Member Zhang are relatives from the same hometown. He does not know the circumstances of his assassination. He was arrested last night while leaving the Jinde Association. The confession is true.

Lin Mingjiu: Confessed that he is 35 years old, from Shewopo Town, south of Qixia County. He is a replacement executive member at the Provincial Party Department. Because he bought a ticket to enter the Jinde Association, he went to play in front of the 22nd Division Recreational Association and watched a play at the Jingju Theater. People were not allowed to enter or leave. He does not know what happened and was arrested later. When he arrived at the Committee Room, he heard that all personnel from the Provincial Party Department were not allowed to leave. He knows nothing about Committee Member Zhang. The confession is true.

Silver and Money Industries Held a Joint Meeting Yesterday After Reopening

Summary Accounting and Silver Coin Transportation Requests for Facilitation

Further Consultation Today Before Visiting Finance Minister Kong for Request

After the New Year holiday, money exchanges and banks reopened on the previous two days. Yesterday at 4:00 PM, a joint meeting of the executive committees of both associations was held to discuss the issue of facilitating the transportation of silver coins during summary accounting. Details are as follows:

Reopening Dates

Money exchanges, members of the Money Exchange Association, resumed operations on the day before yesterday, following established regulations for a two-day New Year holiday. A general meeting resolved that February 3rd would be the summary accounting date for the 23rd year of the Republic of China. Banks, members of the Banking Association, resumed operations yesterday morning, following association regulations for a three-day New Year holiday, and resumed normal business. Simultaneously, the Banking Joint Preparatory Committee and the Clearing House also resumed normal operations yesterday.

Joint Meeting

Yesterday at 4:00 PM, the Banking and Money Exchange Associations held a joint executive committee meeting at the Banking Association on Hong Kong Road. Present were all committee members, including Chen Guangfu and Xu Qizhi from the banks, Qin Runqing and Yu Zuoting from the money exchanges, as well as Qin Xiqing and Lin Kanghou, the secretaries-general of both associations. The chairman first reported that the money exchange summary accounting was set for February 3rd. At that time, various businesses would need a significant amount of silver coins for settlement. Since the Ministry of Finance stipulated that a permit was required to transport silver, transportation would be quite inconvenient. It was decided on the spot to request the Ministry of Finance to facilitate the procedures for transporting silver coins during summary accounting. The meeting adjourned around 5:00 PM.

Visiting Finance Minister Kong

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency learned from the Banking and Money Exchange industries yesterday that the two industry associations would hold another consultation today. Then, each association would appoint committee members to jointly visit Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi and state that various businesses would need a significant amount of cash for settlement during the summary accounting of the 23rd year of the Republic of China. They would request facilitation of procedures for transporting silver coins and offer suggestions for adoption and implementation.

The Future of China National Aviation Corporation Is Very Promising

Achievements of the Past Year 23

And Progress Plans for This Year

China National Aviation Corporation's gradual progress in the past year 23 has been detailed in this newspaper. A comparison of the company's operating income from its establishment in 1929 to the end of 1934 shows that passenger traffic has increased by 50%, and mail transport has increased to 20%. Comparing the income situation over the years, its rapid progress has created a momentum of rapid advancement in China's new aviation industry, and the future is very promising. The reporter inquired with the company yesterday, and details are as follows:

Adding New Aircraft

Starting January 8, 1935, the company will change the Shanghai-Guangdong flights to fly from Shanghai to Guangdong every Tuesday and Friday and return from Guangdong to Shanghai every Thursday and Sunday. The existing Douglas aircraft may not be sufficient, so the company has purchased the largest new aircraft from the United Aircrafts Corporation in the United States. This aircraft can accommodate sixteen people and has an average speed of 290 kilometers per hour. If there is a need to increase flights on this route this year, it will be added to facilitate passenger traffic in South China. In addition to the Stinson aircraft currently used on the Shanghai-Beijing route, the company plans to add a Douglas transport aircraft with two-way wireless communication and the safest equipment. This aircraft flies at 290 kilometers per hour, can accommodate fourteen passengers, and is safe and perfectly equipped. The current flight time on the Shanghai-Beijing route is eight hours, but with this aircraft, it can be reached in about four and a half hours. The company is also preparing the Chongqing-Kunming route and has decided to use Ford aircraft specifically for this route. These aircraft have been ordered and will soon be transported to Shanghai. The aircraft has three engines and is perfectly equipped, and flying is very safe. The company has decided to purchase four Fairchild aircraft for the existing Loening aircraft used on the Hankou-Chongqing route. This type of aircraft is very suitable for flying in the Yangtze River basin. The aircraft is equipped with a two-way wireless communication device and two engines. The aircraft has a speed of approximately 250 kilometers per hour and can accommodate six passengers, making flying very safe.

Trial Flights on New Routes

The company is currently planning the Chongqing-Kunming route, which will allow direct access from Shanghai to Kunming, Yunnan, opening up the most convenient transportation in the southwest. However, the voyage is long, with many mountains and harsh climates. The company is making extremely cautious preparations. The company has first installed many wireless radio stations and has ordered the latest Ford aircraft from the United Aircrafts Corporation in the United States, specifically for this route.

Land Route Exploration

The company feels that the route from Batang to Lhasa is more difficult to plan than the Chongqing-Kunming route. Installing radio stations and expanding airports cannot be predetermined by sending aircraft for trial flights first. Therefore, it has been decided to send personnel by land to start on-site investigations in these two places. After the investigation is accurate, the route and landing locations can be determined. This procedure is currently being planned and will be implemented this year.

Expanding the Airport

The company believes that the original Longhua Airport is narrow, making it extremely inconvenient for larger aircraft to land and take off. Since the decision was made last year to expand the airport, the Ministry of Transportation has sent personnel to assist in renting and purchasing private land to expand the base. Mayor Wu of Shanghai has also provided strong assistance. The issue of expanding the area has been completed. In the future, the difficult situation of larger aircraft landing and taking off in Longhua can be avoided. The company's General Manager, Dai Enji, expressed gratitude for Mayor Wu's assistance to reporters. The company's operating income from 1929 to the end of December 1934 is listed below:

China Pilot Association Preparatory Committee Strives to Revise New Regulations

The Right to Pilotage Is the Most Important Measure for National Defense. Last September, China promulgated Pilotage Regulations to abolish the old regulations of the seventh year of Tongzhi. However, foreign customs officials were the first to oppose it and demand revision. The government has agreed to hand over the recovery of pilotage affairs to the Director-General of Customs. It has now been agreed to prepare a price of 1 million customs taels (equivalent to more than 1.9 million silver dollars) to purchase all the assets and shares of foreign Shanghai pilotage shipping companies and the Shanghai Pilotage Association and revise them. The new regulations will also be announced soon. The content still allows foreigners to serve, and the right to pilotage management is still exclusively in the hands of the customs. The Preparatory Committee of the Chinese Pilot Association in Shanghai believes that this kind of recovery is no different from the previous foreign occupation. The crisis of China's recovery of pilotage has reached the final stage. The situation is urgent. Therefore, a telegram was sent to the National Government to strive for it, which roughly stated (Secretly investigating that the foreign advisers of the customs opposed the recovery of pilotage sovereignty and demanded the revision of the pilotage regulations. The association had already sent a micro-telegram on the 5th of this month to Chen, requesting the chairman to not fall into the trap of traitors in order to protect national rights. Please invite your observation. According to foreign news, the foreign advisers' request has been determined by the Executive Yuan to have four principles, which are handed over to the Ministry of Finance to follow and revise: (1) Abolish the Pilotage Management Committee and change it to customs management, (2) Preserve the positions of old pilots and the assets of the pilotage shipping company, (3) Adopt a compulsory pilotage system, and the pilotage license will be issued by the Ministry of Finance, (3) Purchase the foreign pilotage industry and handle it by the Director-General of Customs. This kind of new regulations has already been drafted and is seeking the opinions of the Director-General of Customs. Once it is approved, it can be published and named Provisional Regulations, etc. It is hereby pointed out that the foreign advisers have long had various conspiracies to destroy the recovery of pilotage. Referring to the conversation between British Minister Cade Gan and our foreign affairs department on March 19 this year, his hopes and the letter from the Shanghai Pilot Association to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, requesting three points, and the Pilotage Management Committee, (omitted) and the gradual reorganization of the pilotage plan by Claire Keick, the private property secretary of the Director-General of Customs, the active figures who are obstructing it have become clear. The regulations that were promulgated in September last year and have not yet been implemented, what is so inconvenient that they have to be changed so quickly? The government's recovery of pilotage was originally based on national defense and military power as a prerequisite, but now the focus of the four principles is not on this. In essence, we already have a feeling of disappointment. Or if we carefully analyze it, there are many loopholes and suspicious points. If we are not careful, we will lose national rights in the future, and it will definitely be worse than the old regulations of the seventh year of Tongzhi. Because since the foreign advisers have served as the Director-General of Customs in our country, the accumulated habits have continued, and the tail is too big to be cut off. The government has no power to command foreign officials, and it has become openly daring to threaten to revise the regulations. This has been going on for a long time. Today, the foreign advisers' request has been complacent, and whether our national rights have been lost, the association's foolishness, I think there is still room for discussion. It is heard that the revised new regulations, regarding the nationality of the pilot, in addition to the existing foreign pilots, will still be preserved. In the future, although the replacement will be limited to Chinese, it is still allowed to be supplemented by foreigners when necessary. What is the difference between changing the soup and not changing the medicine, and the foreign customs officials can use this point at will to deny the qualifications of Chinese to supplement pilotage, and there is a possibility of creating a necessary situation at any time, and continue to use their usual tricks to exclude Chinese and borrow talents from other countries. If you say that you will recover pilotage with this, it will never be realized one day. This is the first thing to consider. Examination is one of the five powers. The pilotage examination should be executed by the Examination Yuan. There is no reason to hand it over to foreigners. Looking at the old regulations of the seventh year of Tongzhi, the election examination was controlled by foreigners. After one year, all Chinese were eliminated, which can be used as a warning. This is the second thing to consider. If the right to manage is controlled by the foreign advisers, even if we can test in the future, the right to appoint and employ is still in the hands of foreigners. Is it in a situation of testing and not using, and existing in name only? This is the third thing to consider. The new regulations of the Shanghai Pilot Association of Foreigners, since it is allowed to exist, then the Chinese pilot in the future will inevitably join the Foreign Association, which is still dominated by foreigners and the Chinese are vassals. There are many obstacles in it. Otherwise, pilotage is a public business and should be organized into a public association. The Chinese can form their own association here, so that the foreigners can be merged into our side. This is the proper way. Does the new regulations take this into account? This is the fourth thing to consider. As for compulsory pilotage, all countries have this system for dangerous harbors and waterways, but this is to preserve the secrets of a country's waterways, entrust the ears and eyes to the people, and obtain national defense guarantees. The law is perfect. Foreign pilotage in our country has not been abolished, so there is no fundamental talk of compulsory pilotage. Now they want to imitate Dong Shi forcibly and entrust the ears and eyes to foreigners. Isn't it a great joke in the world? This is the fifth thing to consider. Since the national crisis, four provinces have been lost, and the shipping industry has been directly affected and has been on the verge of bankruptcy in recent years. Rescuing shipping merchants is one of the important proposals of this year's transportation conference. Why is the relief not being carried out, but instead following the will of the foreign customs officials and implementing compulsory pilotage, which increases the burden on the people? It has not been done through legislative procedures, nor has it sought the consent of the shipping merchants. What is the balance between reason and law? This is the sixth thing to consider. Pilotage is a specialized skill, the same as lawyers and accountants, and is a kind of free business. It is not a government civil servant, and the government cannot use this to make profits, and use the pilot as a tool to open up bad precedents and hinder the people's livelihood. The government has never been able to freely use the customs surplus tons of banknotes handled by the customs, as well as various fines. If compulsory pilotage is implemented, the future pilotage surplus will naturally be the same as the customs surplus and will be arbitrarily distributed by the customs. Isn't this sucking the people's blood to satisfy the foreigners' desires? This is the seventh thing to consider. Furthermore, the proposal for compulsory pilotage was initiated by the customs in the eleventh year of the Republic of China. Their intention was to increase the burden on Chinese shipping merchants and increase the income of foreign pilotage associations. A small part of this would be allocated to hire a few Chinese pilots to ease the Chinese atmosphere. However, the Chinese salary was only set at one-fourth of that of foreigners, and the remaining subsidies were used by foreigners to reduce the pilotage fees for foreign ships. The trick can be said to be impeccable. This is the eighth thing to consider. The old regulations of the seventh year of Tongzhi were submitted by Hede and approved by the Prime Minister's Office for implementation. From top to bottom, it still does not lose its system and majesty. Our revolutionary government originally had the right to recover. Why do we have to bend over and ask for advice on the customs' request to revise the regulations, and gradually cause the emperor to step down? Even if the government intends to compromise, what about the national system? Moreover, the customs has always advocated that the recovery of pilotage must be approved by the diplomatic corps. Now that the customs' proposal is being listened to, it is a tacit agreement, and the situation is as bad as making a cocoon and binding oneself. The association is not smart, and I am afraid that pilotage will be trapped in a never-ending place from now on. This is the ninth thing to consider. Also, the regulations are said to be provisional, which is intended to reserve room for Liu Dingzheng to correct. However, the old regulations of the seventh year of Tongzhi were also provisional, and the Chinese suffered for 66 years. How should we carefully formulate laws and regulations to ensure everything is safe? It must be known that the customs has foreign debt compensation relations. The Director-General of Customs is the supervisory representative of the creditors in the eyes of foreigners. Pre-event consultation is tantamount to seeking a tiger's skin, causing diplomatic disputes and hindering the power to legislate in the future. On the one hand, it still uses the name of provisional to shirk responsibility. This is the tenth thing to consider. Reading (omitted) Director Wang of the Executive Yuan's report on the National Government Memorial Week said, "During the period of political tutelage, we must train the people to exercise political power. During the period of constitutional government, the people's training has matured and they can exercise political power." One is being trained, and the other is trained to maturity. The need for the expression of the people's power and intention is the same. The truth is clear and in line with the meaning of the people as the foundation of the country. The association takes the position of the people. Regardless of whether the foreign news is true or false, the above ten points are of great importance and are purely for the love of the country and for the expression of the people's power and intention. The government can accommodate the demands of the tax affairs department to the outside world, and it should also respect public opinion internally to show fairness. For this reason, I request that your government must first hand over the new regulations revised by the Ministry of Finance this time to the Legislative, Examination, and Judicial Yuan for review in accordance with the established regulations before they are approved and announced, and then implement them. On one hand, transfer the Legislative Yuan to formulate laws and regulations to make them permanent. On the other hand, please send the revised new regulations to the association so that it can jointly discuss and study the pros and cons with the relevant pilotage groups. There will be a thousand thoughts and one gain to offer as a humble contribution for selection. I hope you will consider and approve the request. I am extremely panicked and waiting for orders.

The Private Postal Bureau Is Still Operating

The Public Security Bureau Sent Personnel to Investigate Yesterday

According to the China News Agency, in order to unify the national postal administration, the Ministry of Transportation specifically instructed the Postal Administration last year to order all private postal bureaus across the country to end operations at the end of the year, and to request the local military and police to persuade them to stop operating at that time. However, the national private postal bureau industry has repeatedly petitioned the central government because it affects the lives of more than 100,000 employees, but to no avail. It is now learned that the industry has hired lawyer Zheng Zhenquan to present three reasons based on the law and has filed an administrative appeal with the Ministry of Transportation. However, due to the New Year holiday, the ministry has not yet approved it. Therefore, the industry has decided to continue operating before the Ministry of Transportation has decided on a proper solution. It is heard that the municipal government authorities ordered the private postal bureaus in Beijing and Zhenjiang to close down. Therefore, yesterday, the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent personnel to persuade the private postal bureaus to comply with the order. The industry representatives explained in detail the difficulties in closing down. The personnel agreed to return to the bureau to report the investigation.

Polish School Ship

Has Arrived in Honolulu

Arriving in Yokohama on February 18

The Polish school ship "Great Pomeranian", donated by the people of the Polish Pomeranian Province, is a steel-plated sailing ship equipped with a huge awning. The interior is also equipped with a motor engine, but it is agreed that the voyage must rely entirely on wind power. The motor is not turned on unless it is absolutely necessary. It is about 78.5 meters long, 13.5 meters wide, and has a deadweight of 1,566 tons. The form is extremely beautiful. It set sail from the port of Dai Niya in Poland on September 16 last year and made a grand voyage around the world. The route includes Copenhagen in Denmark, Krus, Santo Domingo, Gulong Islands, Panama Canal, Honolulu, Yokohama, Kobe, Nagasaki in Japan, Shanghai and Hong Kong in China, Singapore and Batavia in the Nanyang Islands, Cape Town in South Africa, St. Helena, Azores Islands, and finally Dover in England before returning to Poland. The estimated journey will be completed around September 1 this year. The ship has 41 staff members, professors, and lecturers, and 66 students from the Maritime School, for a total of 107 people. The captain, named Mosik Weiqi, is very experienced in sailing. All the work on the ship is allocated and operated by these 66 students. At the same time, teachers teach various merchant marine nautical knowledge. After the voyage is completed, the course will also be completed, and they will be assigned to various merchant ships to work. According to the message from the Polish Embassy yesterday, the ship has arrived in Honolulu and is expected to arrive in Yokohama around February 18, and then temporarily park in Nagasaki to repair the ship. It takes about six days to come to Shanghai from Nagasaki, relying entirely on wind power.

The Ministry of Finance Telegraphs Fujian Province to Abolish Harsh Miscellaneous Wood Taxes

According to the New Voice News Agency, the representatives of the fir wood industry in Fujian Province went to Nanjing to petition for the abolition of illegal harsh miscellaneous taxes, which has been reported in previous newspapers. The Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance paid special attention to this. They had already telegraphed the Fujian Provincial Government to investigate and reply. The Fujian Provincial Government stated that the Shuikou Defense Fee, created by Cai Tingkai, which was 45 yuan per company, should be abolished. However, due to the current extreme financial difficulties, it must be implemented slowly. The Zhuzaki Business Tax (actually a transit tax) created by He Gonggan was listed as a legitimate tax and requested for record. The competent authorities of the Ministry of Finance believe that the government's collection of donations and taxes must take into account the cultivation of tax sources. If harsh miscellaneous taxes that hinder production are allowed to exist, the government's temporary tax revenue will increase. However, due to the decline in both agricultural and commercial production and sales, the legitimate revenue will be sharply reduced, which is tantamount to a suicidal policy of draining the pond to get all the fish. They telegraphed the provincial government to quickly abolish the Shuikou Defense Fee and correct the heavy Zhuzaki Business Tax.

Preparation Progress of the Central Machine Manufacturing Plant

The Central Machine Manufacturing Plant of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce held a foundation stone laying ceremony in Shanghai on New Year's Day. The establishment of this plant is a key day for the future development of industry. The following is a record of the plant's preparation progress:

The government's desire to establish this plant dates back several years. The purpose is to enable the country to manufacture its own machines used in various industries, to prevent waste, and to implement the plan to realize Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings to develop industry and solve people's livelihoods. It is heard that the start-up cost requires more than 3 million yuan. At a time of financial difficulties, it is not easy to raise this large sum of money. However, in order to implement this policy, the ministry has reached an agreement with the Central Gengkuan Committee. After deliberation by the Central Political Conference, it was approved to borrow a part of the funds from the committee, and the rest will be raised by the ministry itself. This is the source of funds. The next step is to survey the plant site. Caoxie Gorge in Nanjing was once identified as the plant base, but it was not suitable, so another plant site had to be selected. Because the plant's funds are borrowed, it must be able to repay the debt after it is opened. The selection of the plant site must take into account the supply of raw materials, the sales market, and water and land transportation. Shanghai is the center of industry and commerce, and rail transportation is extremely convenient. Setting up a plant here is most suitable. In particular, the selection of workers is easier than in other places. Therefore, after careful consideration, the ministry decided to set up a plant in Shanghai. There was land for sale in Beixinjing, facing Zhenbei Road in the front and connecting to the Suzhou River in the back, which is located between the Nanjing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways. In the future, the plant's internal tracks can be connected to the two railways, and the automobile road can directly reach the city center. Water and land transportation is most suitable. Previously, the plant organized a preparatory office in Nanjing and sent Situ Xi, the deputy director of the office, to various provinces to investigate the machine needs in various places and the location of raw material production. Then, based on the social needs and the principle of competing with different small factories, the types of products were determined. There are many types of machines, and the types of machines needed in our country are also very complex. Therefore, we must distinguish between urgency and priority and define the scope of manufacturing as three major categories: prime movers, machine tools, and hardware parts. The parts, such as pig iron pipes, seamless steel pipes, and pipe parts, cast iron, cast steel, screws, white iron sheets, and black iron sheets, etc., are all in huge demand in society. In the future, when the plant starts operation, it will be very beneficial to recover rights and interests. Last year, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce also sent Lu Weipu, the director of the office, to various countries in Europe and the West to investigate the latest manufacturing methods and then determine the machines to be purchased. It is heard that the purchase of materials is based on the principle of being the most economical and efficient, so as to save start-up costs. It is also prepared to manufacture a variety of machines and machine parts when expanding in the future. It is also heard that the plant's factory building design uses steel materials for the factory part and adopts the latest European and American methods, so that the transportation of raw materials and finished products during manufacturing follows the shortest and most convenient flow line to increase efficiency. The factory building area is mostly factory, and the office is only a small part. Since the plant's site was changed to Shanghai, the preparatory office has also moved from Nanjing to Shanghai for the convenience of office work. It is heard that its recent work has become more tense. The various things it is preparing are to investigate the market needs at any time, the number of machine parts imported each year, the prices, output, and conditions of various raw materials, and plan the plant's future water and electricity supply and equipment, and how to manufacture the products in the factory in the future to obtain excellent results, and how to promote the business to develop well, and how to train workers to make their skills excellent and obtain the highest work efficiency in the shortest time, are all under constant research, so as to be able to obtain the hope of a rapid increase in production after the plant is opened. It is also heard that the Minister of Industry and Commerce, and the Vice Minister, the Director, etc., have high expectations for the plant and supervise it strictly. The method of handling affairs is to make it scientific, the method of business is to make it commercial, and the selection of staff is based on talent, and the training of workers is adapted to the needs, so that the purpose of machine manufacturing can be directly achieved, and the basic industrial plan of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce in the near future can be completed indirectly. Therefore, at the foundation stone laying ceremony on New Year's Day, Minister Chen personally laid the foundation stone, and Vice Minister Liu and Vice Minister Gu also came to the site to guide. It was not grand.

The Yue Railway Bureau has more than 600,000 yuan that has not been allocated to the fund, which adds up to more than 800,000 yuan, which is enough for the first principal repayment. The Endless Stream of Strange and Bizarre Events: Many Old Maids Get Married (Shao Yongnan) Jointly Requesting Relief from the Authorities Choosing Mates Within a Set Time Limit, Faces Showing Delight The authorities in Guangxi province, recently aiming to vigorously develop culture, initiated a survey of popular sentiment. Consequently, strange and bizarre events emerged one after another. The most amusing was that a survey team went to Shangjin County for investigation, starting from Zhongyou Road. The results showed that the total number of women in the county was 455, and the number of unmarried old maids aged 25 to 50 accounted for as many as 200, nearly reaching 50% of the total. At the same time, similar situations existed in other villages and towns. For a time, the name of "old maids" in the county spread far and wide. These old maids, mostly feeling sexual hunger but unable to resolve it, jointly protested against the old families and jointly requested relief measures from the county government. The county government immediately accepted the request and sought ways to provide relief. All virgins aged 25 to over 40 were required to choose a mate within a set time limit; failure to do so would result in a heavy fine. Upon hearing the county government's relief measures, the old maids all showed delight, busying themselves with purchasing new clothes in preparation for marriage. It is heard that a certain merchant from Longzhou County, near the county, has purchased a large number of copper and iron beds from Shunxing Company, the largest copper bed store (Bed King) in Shanghai, and transported them to Guangxi. It is not known whether these goods are for their use after choosing mates. The situation is thought-provoking and truly amusing.

Detailed Record of the Lake Society's Formal Attire Campaign 93

The Lake Society, seeing that the formal attire prescribed by the Ministry of Interior had not been universally adopted and implemented by the public, launched a significant formal attire campaign, advocating the use of domestic silk and other materials as raw materials, which has attracted attention from all sectors of society. After holding a group worship and dinner on New Year's Day, a meeting was convened at 2:00 PM. Over a thousand people attended, and staff from Bingxun Stenography School were sent to record the proceedings. The details of the meeting are recorded below:

Meeting Venue Arrangement At the entrance of the society, a memorial archway made of pine and cypress branches was erected. At the entrance of the second floor, electric lights spelled out the four characters "Formal Attire Campaign," dazzlingly bright. The meeting was held in the Ying Shi Memorial Hall on the second floor. The Party and National flags and the society's flag were inserted on the podium, with a portrait of the late Premier wearing a blue robe and black mandarin jacket hanging in the center to show the purpose to the attendees. The venue was adorned with colorful silks, to promote the significance of silk.

Chairman's Address The chairman of the conference, Shen Tianhua, reported the purpose of the meeting, stating briefly: The difference between civilization and barbarism lies in etiquette, which most easily demonstrates a country's spirit and cultural atmosphere. Since China has been a land of propriety, how can we abandon the word "propriety"? Therefore, in addition to diplomats, military and police officers having separate formal attire regulations, other sectors should also have a uniform formal attire. The Lake Society's launching of the formal attire campaign is, in terms of strength, a mere drop in the ocean, but we believe that if something should be done, we will not refrain from doing it just because our strength is small, simply to make an initial push for the formal attire campaign. As for the formal attire system promulgated by the Ministry of Interior in 1929, it only specifies a blue robe and black mandarin jacket for men, without mentioning the patterns or simplicity of the attire. However, in the opinion of our society, formal attire is meant to demonstrate civilization and should preferably use domestic silk, so as to promote domestic goods. As for women's formal attire, in addition to the blue jacket and black skirt, the currently popular "qipao" (cheongsam) should be corrected to use the character "qi" from "shuo ren qi qi," which also has a meaning for today's formal attire campaign. Currently, the Huzhou Crepe Industry Association and the Wuxing Silk Weaving and Knitting Associations are advertising prizes to solicit formal attire designs, preparing to organize a judging committee to determine standards and submit them to Party and government agencies for approval and implementation. The formal attire worn by this chairman today is a temporary standard. Today's meeting is the beginning of the campaign. I hope that all comrades from all walks of life will work together to achieve the goal of uniform and tidy formal attire. Following this,

Speeches from Various Sectors The Director of the Department of Etiquette and Customs of the Ministry of Interior, Lu Xirong, delivered a speech, stating briefly: Formal attire is closely related to customs and has a great impact on national spirit. The government attaches great importance to this matter. The Lake Society's holding of the formal attire campaign also implies the promotion of domestic silk. Chinese people should wear domestic goods, so that the national economy has hope of recovery. Shanghai is a place of national attention. The formal attire campaign, launched in Shanghai, will surely have a positive impact nationwide. From the habits of 3 million citizens, extended to 400 million compatriots, this is the best approach. I also hope that the formal attire campaign will not only promote national spirit but also promote domestic goods and assist in the development of the national economy. Next, Zhu Xuechun, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, delivered a speech, stating briefly: China has 2,000 years of culture, why is its international status low? The only reason is that progress stalled at a certain point, leading to a state of not knowing what to do. To raise international status, we must first develop inherent cultural morality. Everyone should pay attention to etiquette. To pay attention to etiquette, we must first promote formal attire. Silk is a major Chinese product. The raw materials for formal attire should be domestic silk, because Huzhou is a silk-producing area. Currently, domestic silk is under pressure from foreign artificial silk, becoming more and more serious, leading to the collapse of the silk industry. It is a great mistake for Chinese people not to use domestic goods but to use foreign goods. Next, Qiu Henian, representative of the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, delivered a speech, stating briefly: It is very meaningful to promote formal attire and domestic goods in Shanghai, because every move in Shanghai attracts national attention. As long as the atmosphere in Shanghai changes, the whole country will change. The formal attire campaign should not only promote domestic clothing materials but also all other supplies should use domestic goods. I, as an official in the Trademark Bureau, have felt in the past few years that the output of domestic goods is really too poor. Chinese trademarks are less than one-tenth of foreign trademarks. Now, the variety of domestic goods is increasing daily, enough for the needs of the Chinese people. The previous promotion of domestic goods was merely a response to stimulation and temporary emotional impulse, and it was soon forgotten. Now, domestic goods have all three points of "beauty," "durability," and "cheapness," which are very suitable for the purchasing power of the people. This is the significance of promoting domestic goods in the formal attire campaign. Next, Yan Duhe delivered a speech, stating briefly: Ladies and gentlemen, today is New Year's Day, and everyone has new hopes and new progress. The formal attire campaign, with the meeting held today, especially on New Year's Day, which is full of new progress and new hope, is even more meaningful. The formal attire campaign has two purposes: first, to respect the system, to put it plainly, is to let everyone know etiquette and respect Chinese etiquette; second, to promote formal attire and domestic goods. Let's talk about the first point, why respect etiquette? Of course, formal attire is related to the etiquette of a country. Although it is very simple in history, it is also very clear. In the past, every change of dynasty would first change the "calendar" and then change the clothing colors. Why change the clothing colors? The most important thing is because clothing is very related to the society, the country, and the entire people. Since the establishment of the Republic of China, the "calendar" has been changed and the world's uniform calendar has been adopted, canceling the lunar calendar. When it comes to clothing colors, it has not been changed much. On the one hand, the uniform clothing for diplomats and police has been stipulated; on the other hand, formal attire has been formulated, with black mandarin jackets and blue robes. Although this formal attire has been stipulated, the public has not complied with it. Whether it is weddings, funerals, or dances, the clothes worn are almost the same. This set of clothes is worn at home, and this set is worn to congratulate or mourn. It is really ridiculous. Just like acting, although the role is played in a game, there is a certain costume, and marriage has the color of marriage, and funerals have the appearance of funerals, so that people can know at a glance. Otherwise, wouldn't it be like a clown performing a play, not following certain rules? Our various actions, because we are the parties involved, we don't feel fake ourselves. If we stand as bystanders to see the actions of the Chinese people, when we encounter celebrations or condolences, it is so chaotic, disregarding appearance, and lacking spirit. Even a team of soldiers, if their clothes are messy, we can tell at a glance that they are not a good army. Therefore, the first point of promoting formal attire is to respect etiquette, and the second point is to promote domestic goods. Just now, Mr. Qiu has said that the number of domestic goods has increased day by day. Promoting domestic goods does not necessarily require a formal attire campaign, but the formal attire campaign cannot fail to pay attention to promoting domestic goods. Promoting domestic goods should not only focus on clothing materials, but also on food, we must focus on domestic goods. Using our own domestic goods, silk, is a Chinese thing. China has 400 million people, and counting one-third of the rural farmers, and excluding a part of the poor who don’t wear silk, there are still 100 million to 200 million people who can wear silk. The silk industry is not without a solution. Moreover, the current silk price is extremely cheap, almost some good cloth is more expensive than silk. As long as everyone can use it, there is no worry that silk will not prosper. I hope that the New Year's Day of 1935 is the beginning of this movement, and on the New Year's Day of 1936, we will hold a commemorative meeting for the success of the movement. Next, Mr. Wang Yansong of the Silk Industry Bank said briefly: There have been many actions related to promoting domestic goods in the past, such as the Women's Domestic Goods Year, the Domestic Goods Exhibition, and the Silk Exhibition last year. Now in 1935, we are still promoting domestic goods. Everyone wears formal attire. At the same time, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce also held a Student Domestic Goods Year and a Domestic Goods Exhibition. Many movements in China in the past two years have also achieved much success. On the surface, they have been quite successful. Today's formal attire conference, Mr. Yan Duhe has just said that formal attire is important to individuals, to the nation, and to the country. I have another point, that formal attire is also very important to customs. We wear formal attire, there must be special things, or weddings, or funerals, or banquets, are more important things. Wearing formal attire should wear clothes made of Chinese goods. Today, I met two people with different ones, one is Director Pan, wearing Chinese clothes, which are domestic goods, his robe only costs six yuan, and he wore a suit, which cost one hundred and twenty yuan. Compared, Chinese clothes only cost six yuan, and Western clothes are so much more expensive, so it can be seen that domestic goods are cheaper. Then, from this point of view, imported goods are neither economical nor profitable. It’s better to promote domestic goods. However, the formal attire campaign should lead by example. Yesterday was the New Year's Eve, and there were no dance halls in Hangzhou in Nanshi, so a group of political leaders all ran to Shanghai to enter the dance halls, wearing Western clothes and eating big meals. They refused to earnestly practice it themselves, but called on everyone to use domestic goods. They couldn’t lead by example. If this continues, I’m afraid that domestic goods will be promoted every year, and the import surplus will increase every year. Next, Mr. Wang Xiaolai said briefly: The speaker just now was Mr. Wang Yansong. At this moment, I am speaking, and we are both surnamed Wang, we should do a double act. Everyone should know that the way to do a double act is that one person speaks and one person does, how to say, how to do, if you say and don't do, it's not a double act. We promote formal attire, we must be like a double act, while saying, we must do it, that's right. Today is New Year's Day. When friends see it, they always open their mouths and congratulate you on getting rich. In fact, to get rich, you must first develop your business. Rather than saying congratulations on getting rich, it is better to say congratulations on your business. Otherwise, everyone wants to get rich, there are banks on the market, but no factories, what is it like? No wonder the banks are going bankrupt. Let's talk about formal attire. China is a country of culture and objects. Etiquette, music, archery, writing, and mathematics are literature. Etiquette is the most important. The important place to show etiquette is clothing. Now we promote formal attire, but the felt hats worn on the head and the leather shoes worn on the feet are all foreign goods. Isn't it headless and tailless? Therefore, we promote formal attire and domestic goods, we must thoroughly understand it, and don't be headless and tailless. Next, Mr. Luo Qinghua of the Silk Industry Association made an adjustment, stating briefly: Promoting formal attire is not only the matter of the Lake Society, nor is it only the matter of the silk industry, but the matter of the whole nation. China has had formal attire for a long time. Since the promulgation of the formal attire regulations in 1929, because no one promoted it, it has not been universally implemented in 1935. In fact, formal attire is very important. The so-called tidy clothes and hats, look like a Yan Ran, people look at it and return to it, this is the effect of formal attire. Let's talk about the quality of formal attire, of course silk is needed. Silk is a special product of China. The clothes and hats of the ancestral temples of all dynasties are all made of silk raw materials. Some people say that the blue robe and black mandarin jacket are corruption, this is a slanderous statement. Did Emperor Wu of the Han Dynasty conquer the Western Regions and Yuan Shizu conquer the Great Qin, did they wear suits? Looking at the Japanese, they should be very inconvenient to wear clogs, but one foot has crossed into the four eastern provinces of our country. Chinese people have no self-confidence, like the boss who opens a cigarette factory, they like to eat茄力克 themselves, how can such a move have good results? I am not saying that the three names are inseparable from my profession, promoting domestic goods, we must implement it ourselves to have a way out.
