Zhang Naiqi Speaks on the Evaluation of the New Village Movement On the afternoon of the 3rd of this month at 7:30 PM, the China New Village Construction Society held its first New Village lecture in the auditorium of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA. 480 people attended. Economist Zhang Naiqi spoke on the evaluation of the New Village Movement, briefly stating that although there are many categories of knowledge and research in a society, they are all interconnected as a whole. In the past, researchers of a certain specialized issue often held biased views. Historically speaking, the New Village Movement originated from socialists who advocated utopianism. They wanted to create a new environment without reforming the existing society, hoping to abandon the old environment. However, due to the strong influence of the old environment, the newly created environment was often swallowed up. In the past, the failures of New Village Movement advocates in various countries were mostly due to this. Now, as far as I know, the members of the China New Village Construction Society are very clear about the overly idealistic nature of utopian socialism. The members of the society have realized the realities of urban expansion in economic life and want to solve the housing problem for urban people. They do not use high-sounding slogans such as transforming new societies to promote old societies, but only engage in practical efforts to solve the housing problem and personal economic life for the majority, which is possible. Because the society can enable everyone to take out the amount of consumption equal to living in the city and can turn consumption into appreciation, can periodically obtain real estate ownership and eliminate the burden of indefinite rent, the intention is excellent and the method is very simple, and the living environment is more comfortable, quiet and hygienic than in the city, this is the evaluation of the New Village Movement advocated by the members of the society. In addition, there is another point that can indirectly help urban households who have not joined the New Village, that is, because the New Village Movement advocates that most people are willing to move outside the city, the real estate in the city will inevitably fall in price and the rent will definitely be reduced accordingly, then on the one hand, the New Village residents have already obtained substantial benefits, and on the other hand, the urban residents have obtained more real benefits, which is truly a win-win situation.

Seducing the Elder Sister is Punished Wei Hanchen's daughter, Lian Di, from Anhui, is currently 16 years old. She has been working as an elder sister at the house of Dai Yin, a woman at No. 146, Lane 1238, Fuxi Road. On the afternoon of December 14th of last year, she was suddenly lured by Zeng Yang, a woman from the same hometown, to the house of Xu Yinxun, her lover, at No. 18, Lane 990, Jia Zhi Road in the Nanshi area. That night, Xu forcibly raped Wei. Afterwards, Wei Lian Di sent a letter to her father, who reported it to the Jing'an Temple Police Station. Inspector Ni Jiafeng was dispatched to arrest Zeng Yang, Xu Yinxun, and Wei Lian Di and take them to the First Special Court. After the interrogation was concluded, the two defendants were ordered to be detained for sentencing, and Wei's daughter was allowed to be taken back by her father first. Yesterday morning, the presiding judge Liu Yugui announced the verdict in the Eighth Criminal Court. The main text of the sentence stated that Zeng Yang was sentenced to six months' imprisonment for luring a woman under the age of 20 to leave the person with parental rights, and Xu Yinxun was sentenced to three years and six months' imprisonment for raping a woman under the age of 16. Zeng Yang was acquitted of the charge of assisting in rape, and Xu Yinxun was acquitted of the charge of interfering with the family.

Commercial News, Finance, Exchange Market

Panic Selling Erupts, Standard Gold Plummeted Eleven Yuan

First Due to Mr. Luo's Desperate Selling, Market Weakened

Later, News of Central Bank Intervention Gradually Stabilized

The gold market was closed for three days for the New Year holiday. Yesterday was the first day of trading. Unexpectedly, the extreme hardening of the shilling rate triggered a wave of selling. Speculator Mr. Luo also engaged in desperate selling, leading to a sharp decline. A certain bank took the opportunity to maintain prices at the low end, and the market gradually stabilized after the drop. At the beginning of the morning, during the New Year holiday, overseas silver markets rose, but not significantly. London forward silver actually fell by 1.5 to 1.01 cents, and exchange rates also narrowed. London spot gold rose by seven pence, and sentiment was still good. Off-exchange pre-market trading opened, initially rising to 72.73 yuan. However, Kong Yin, a large seller, took advantage of the high prices to sell, and the price immediately retreated into the 70 yuan range. Although there was some struggle at this point, sentiment had already become weak and fatigued. The oversupply situation was extremely evident. The Central Bank's official exchange rates were announced, with the British pound unchanged and the U.S. dollar down by 0.0625. Customs gold units rose by eight li. The standard gold price was 996.40 yuan. Sentiment was unmoved. The market opened lower in the morning. Buyers took advantage of the low prices to become active, briefly pushing the price close to the 70 yuan mark. Although HSBC supported the shilling, it was difficult to rise further because the Jewish merchant Qiao Zhifu was on the verge of collapse. Large sellers jointly sold off at the high prices, and there was a lack of buyers. The exchange market also loosened. Under the pressure of the selling wave, the gold price declined. Banks continued to support the market, but there was still some struggle after the drop. Subsequently, the Central Bank and the Bank of Japan successively offered gold, and the exchange market hardened, but it was still difficult to maintain. Many large long position holders also came out to sell, and the price broke through the 60 yuan mark. The silver equalization tax was announced and remained unchanged, still levied at 6.25%. The British exchange rate was calculated at one shilling and five pence and seventy-five. Although the market stabilized slightly at this point, Yuan Maoyong's repeated selling put further pressure on the buyers' side, and the downward trend remained strong. However, there were still many who took advantage of the low prices to buy, and individual investors followed suit one after another, making efforts to support the market. Therefore, even though large sellers continued to offer gold after that, the overall trend turned stable. However, it was difficult to sustain above 60 yuan. At noon, the exchange market had stabilized, and the gold market was also slightly healthier. Although the afternoon market opened flat, Sassoon, a Western merchant, unexpectedly dumped shillings, causing the domestic market to harden further. Speculator Mr. Luo continued to sell aggressively. Unfavorable rumors spread, and the price declined. A certain bank stepped in to buy, and buyers in the market also took advantage of the low prices to become active. Buying sentiment gradually recovered. Although there was some struggle along the way, the price gradually rebounded due to the enthusiastic buying and the sellers' covering their short positions. Indian silver, on the other hand, declined slightly. After entering the market, the price actually rebounded to above the 60 yuan mark. There was still a lot of supply at the high prices, and the price retreated slightly. Thereafter, the banks' appetite fluctuated between selling and supporting, and the exchange market stabilized. Buyers were active from time to time, and the market situation was quite stable, but it was difficult to break through the 60 yuan mark. In the end, supply and demand balanced, and the situation did not change significantly, resulting in a stagnant outcome. The day's market situation is recorded below:

Exchange Rate Decline Triggers British Exchange Selling

Central Bank, Qiao Zhifu, and Sassoon All Sell

Tian Exchange Market Results in Both British and U.S. Hardening

The exchange market was closed for three days for the New Year holiday. During this period of market closure, overseas telegrams indicated that London large bars rose by 0.0625 for both near and far terms, U.S. silver rose by 125, and the forward price of Montriuli fell by 1.5 to 1.05 cents. London spot gold rose by seven pence, the British pound fell against the U.S. dollar by 0.625, the U.S. dollar fell against the British pound by 1.625, the British pound fell against the French franc by 50 points, and the U.S. dollar rose against the French franc by 0.3125. The morning opening price for near-term selling was one shilling, four pence, and 8125, and for the U.S. dollar, 34.5625 yuan, which was unchanged for the British pound and tighter by 125 for the U.S. dollar compared to before the market closure, due to the decline in the exchange rate. The Central Bank's official exchange rates were announced, with the British pound unchanged and the U.S. dollar down by 0.0625, and customs gold rose by eight li. Sentiment was depressed after the opening, and Jewish merchants and others sold, causing the market to harden. However, because banks were still supporting, HSBC's official exchange rates were announced, with the British pound unchanged and the U.S. dollar down by 125, and there was still some fluctuation. The Central Bank and the Bank of Japan continued to supply, resulting in oversupply. Although the silver equalization tax was unchanged, the domestic market continued to harden. In the end, banks traded with each other, and the market stabilized slightly at noon. In the afternoon, Sassoon suddenly dumped shillings, and although banks had an appetite for buying, the situation loosened again due to oversupply. After the Opening of the Silver and Money Industry

The Money Supply Remains Tight

After the New Year holiday, the money industry resumed business the day before yesterday (the 3rd), and most of the banks reopened yesterday (the 4th). According to market conditions on the 3rd, foreign exchange rates were 0.55, the same as before the New Year. Yesterday's market also added water to the clearing, making the procedures extremely cumbersome. Many banks were suspected of settling accounts, so the market was more attractive than before the New Year. The opening price was initially 0.5, then changed to 0.6, and finally changed to 0.58, indicating that the tight money supply had not eased slightly. In terms of discount trading, the morning session had over 3.1 million in transfer accounts and over 2.3 million in new transactions. The afternoon session had over 300,000 in transactions. The small general association had over 800,000 in transactions. The total amount of foreign exchange collateral transactions, including withdrawals and new transactions, was about 2 million. In terms of bank settlements, foreign banks settled over 5.7 million in ticket payments, over 8.3 million in various exchange goods collateral payments, electronic settlements, and miscellaneous payments, over 5.3 million in supplementary handling of various payments during the market closure period, over 900,000 in special exchange payments, and 800,000 in warehouse entries. Securities and Bond Market Constrained by Tight Money Supply

Yesterday, the Chinese Securities Exchange was the first red day of the 24th year. After a five-day holiday, there were no changes in the environment, but the foreign exchange rate did not ease, so sentiment could not be boosted. However, the trading volume in the market was not enthusiastic. The atmosphere was sluggish, and the market situation was depressed. Initially, the market was firm due to buying by numbers 50 and 53, but then weakened due to selling by the North Gang numbers 11 and 21. The overall trend remained weak. Although the bulls intended to raise prices, they lacked the strength to do so. As the Lunar New Year approached, the foreign exchange rate was not likely to ease in the short term. The rumor that HSBC would bring back 20 million was not realized, so the prospects were not promising in the short term. Yesterday's performance showed that individual investors sold heavily in the morning session due to the tight money supply. Buyers only included numbers 50 and 53, who had some appetite, so the market price was only firm in the front rows, and weakened further back. The tax-included forward price suddenly fell by half a yuan. The second session was slightly chaotic, with sparse entries and exits. The market situation was uncertain, with highs and lows fluctuating by about 0.2 to 0.3 yuan. In the afternoon, the clearing was done at 0.6 yuan, and sentiment turned weak. The North Gang sold more heavily, and number 21 also dumped, with the gold short position falling sharply by 0.45 yuan, and the rest also consistently fell by about 0.2 to 0.3 yuan. Before the close, the front rows made up for the decline by 0.2 to 0.45 yuan, and the back rows were stable. Cotton Yarn and Gold Prices Fall, Yarn Market Attempts to Rise but Declines

In the mediation office, the district chief sat on the rattan chair in the center, with the landlord and the gold panners sitting opposite each other on both sides. District Chief! What kind of world is this?) The landlord, looking very agitated, said in a tense and hurried voice. (They are still acting recklessly, even using soil to bury the rice seedlings to death.) (Why are you being so unreasonable? The government has already issued a decree prohibiting the use of tax fields and forests. Don't you know that you are breaking the law? Even if... you should ask your conscience, can you live with it?) The district chief questioned the gold panners. (Why don't you go panning in the barren hills and wastelands?) (Yes, we've panned in the barren hills and wastelands, but there's nothing there. The gold just happens to be in the fields. We can't help it. Although we've seen the notice, we're afraid of starving to death... we still have our families to feed?) (District Chief, you must punish them.) (Breaking the law should be punished, do you understand?) the district chief said. (District Chief! For the sake of conscience and to survive, we pan for gold.) (Besides panning for gold, can't you make a living? So many people don't pan for gold, and they don't all starve to death.) (Panning for gold is the same as working. It shows that we're not unwilling to work, but when we look for work, no one wants to hire us. No one buys firewood or grass. In these long days of May, we're starving for days.) said the gold panner. (Now our gold beds and gold buckets have been smashed by them. District Chief! These are our lives. We hope the District Chief will uphold justice and make them pay compensation.) (Our fields, our rice, how will you compensate us?) The district chief pondered for a moment, his temper flaring up a bit; (Other people's tax fields have to pay grain and taxes and are protected by law. You openly dig them up, have you paid any compensation? Do you think that only your gold beds and gold buckets are protected by special laws?) (But those are our lives.) ... Knowing that such disputes are unsolvable, the district chief had no choice but to resort to the established law, the "one strike, two separate" method: (Alright! There's no need for either side to say more, everyone disperse. You must not pan in tax fields again in the future.)

Casual Words from the Study: Philosopher 94

On Knowledge and Concepts

Knowledge originates from the understanding of objective existence, that is, the acquisition of concepts; knowledge is nothing more than the gathering, analysis, and categorization of concepts to discover their commonality and particularity, and to discover the laws of the movement of things through the relationships between concepts. Therefore, the quantity of knowledge depends on the quantity of concepts, and the quality of knowledge is determined by the quality of concepts. To make our knowledge rich and accurate, we must first make our concepts rich and accurate, so examining the process of acquiring concepts would not be superfluous. The acquisition of concepts is usually due to experience and books, and the path is sensation and reflection. We acquire the concept of white through the response of the visual nerve to white, and similarly acquire concepts such as triangle, fragrance, and speed through the sensation's response to the breadth, nature, and movement of things; at the same time, we acquire the concept of man, the concept of existence and entity, and all other higher-level complex concepts through reflection. The vagueness of our concepts affects the clarity of knowledge, and the fragmentation and incompleteness of our concepts also make our knowledge lack a system, which is the most common mistake we make. Why do we have vague and fragmented concepts? Partly due to congenital defects in sensory perception, and partly due to the inability to concentrate attention. A person who is born deaf will never be able to acquire the concept of musical scales and timbres, and therefore will not have musical knowledge; if he can have knowledge of sound, he will acquire it from books, recite it, and it will not be knowledge that is knowledge. Strictly speaking, it is impossible for a person who has no concept of sound at all to read and memorize the definitions and principles in an introduction to music, right? Even if he reads it reluctantly, he will not understand its meaning. Can that still be considered knowledge? As for a person who is born nearsighted, his concept of stars and celestial bodies will naturally be very vague or even incorrect. Such a person, no matter how many books on astronomy he reads, will still be unable to become an astronomer. However, if a person with healthy senses is inattentive, he will neglect many concepts within a system, thus lacking many intermediate concepts, and his knowledge cannot but be fragmented, or even if it is not fragmented, it cannot but be vague. This is especially true when acquiring knowledge from books. We often read books very casually, without seeking to understand the concepts provided by the books, or even wanting to remember them at all, and later, when reading more advanced books, we are unable to understand the ideas within. In addition to these two errors, we also have faulty memory and faulty judgment, both of which are enough to distort our knowledge. We often link unrelated concepts together because of errors in memory and errors in judgment. The reason why great thinkers can discover the truth is because of the clarity of their memory and the clarity of their judgment, so that all concepts have a correct connection. When a person completely loses memory and judgment, his concepts are linked together in a very strange way, and he becomes insane. If we want to make our concepts rich and correct, we must constantly acquire new concepts, often concentrate our attention on concepts, cultivate memory and judgment, arrange concepts in a correct system, and maintain appropriate relationships.

The Mind of an Old Man: Xi Si 95

(I feel more and more desolate, the mind of an old man who is not yet old!) Recently, I often inexplicably sigh to myself like this. Then, in an instant, I ask myself again: I am still young, why does my soul feel so dim? But I cannot say the reason why, I just clearly know that my mind is getting older day by day. The intense attachment and interest of young people have completely disappeared. Therefore, I am dragging a young body but not a young, old heart, trudging along. Because of the dimness of my mind, all the people and things, all the scenery displayed before my eyes are also covered with a layer of dim color. Therefore, I particularly like a solitary and lonely life, often alone, all day long, guarding in a small room, pacing back and forth. Sometimes I walk to the window, look up at the shadows of the clouds in the sky, lightly sketching various beautiful patterns, silently gazing for a long time. As dusk approaches, this natural scenery is another kind of attachment. The sunset drags the tired, light rays of the sun, dyeing red a corner of the western sky, and gilding the distant woods. At this time, perhaps a flock of returning crows occasionally flies across the sky, heavily throwing down a string of desolate cries, which in this desolate and peaceful dusk, heavily falls into my delicate nerves. After the color of night has completely painted down, I silently close the window. I use such a lonely mood to accompany a lonely mind, passing the days in such loneliness. My mind is really old. If I don't have to step out of the door, I can spend a long time without leaving this room. Every day, from morning to night, I look at the clouds in the sky, look at the evening scenery at sunset. Although the situation is somewhat similar to the desolate atmosphere of an ancient temple, I am precisely fascinated by such a desolate, yet elegant and beautiful situation. I would rather spend long days confined in a small room, letting boundless loneliness lock me in. Let loneliness, like a worm, quietly gnaw at my soul. I don't want to mix in crowded and bustling places, laughing because others laugh, and rejoicing because others rejoice. What makes me particularly embarrassed is when I hear something that seems to contain infinite concern and sigh for me, saying: You seem older these days! You should take a break. When these words enter my ears, I have no regret. My old mind cannot be understood by others! When I am old, I should have the golden dreams and golden ideals that young people have. But now I have none of them, not even the smallest hope. I just watch helplessly as the venomous god of fate tramples on the petals of my youth, waiting for my youth, which has never been brilliant, to gradually wither away. In this way, I use my old mind, without emotional prolongation, to pass the years. Seeing the yellow leaves falling, I know that autumn has come. Hearing the orioles whispering in the flowers, I know that late spring is near. Each season comes and goes in a hurry, but these have nothing to do with me. There is no spring and no autumn. I only have a stagnant, never-ending, faded, old mind!

Wife's Transformation: A Le 96

My wife's recent behavior is really hard to figure out. Sometimes she seems quite happy, repeatedly talking about the scenes of a few years ago when we were completely immersed in the trap of love, talking and talking, and finally, she would pounce on me and bite me. But sometimes she is so depressed, lying in bed, sleeping all day long. If I ask her: (Are you feeling unwell?) She always shakes her head and says: (No.) (Then why are you sleeping all day?) (If I'm not sleepy, what's the point?) (Go out and play for a while, don't sleep yourself sick.) I walk over and sit on the edge of the bed. She turns over, faces inward, pulls the quilt over her head, and says: (Nag, nag, nag, I want to sleep.) My wife has really become very strange recently. Her cold face is gradually increasing, and she always sneaks out alone when I go to the company. When I ask her where she is going, she always speaks hesitantly. Either a friend from the north is coming to meet her, or a relative is coming to find her to go to the cinema together. If I ask further what the relative's name is or where the friend lives, she stares at the ceiling, thinks for a while, and then says it. She went out again today. According to the usual practice, today is particularly busy, and I usually don't come back until around 7 or 8 pm. But today is an exception. The company doesn't have that much work to do, so I came back a little earlier. Maybe she still thinks I'm buried in work! I sit alone in the house, as if sitting on pins and needles. My heart feels strangely anxious, and a kind of unbearable shame immediately floats into my mind. Angrily, I slam the table with my hand and curse: (Damn it, she's hooking up with a man.) But I immediately regret it, cursing myself for not speculating on my own wife like that. In any case, she would not abandon me. If she were to abandon me today, there would not have been so much love for me back then. Thinking of this, my anxious and angry mood slowly relaxes. However, the short hand of the clock on the table is running forward quickly, and the sky is also darkening, but she has not yet returned. Where did she go? I start to feel anxious again. The thought that I had just cursed myself for not speculating on her like that is now shaken. I suddenly remember that I can always find some evidence from her clothes pocket or drawer, so I open the wardrobe, rummage around in her cheongsams and blouses for a while, pull out the drawer, search it, and finally find nothing. Just at this moment, she comes in. She sees the clothes scattered on the chair and the drawer open, and the clever her immediately understands what I mean. (Why are you searching everywhere?) Her face has no goodwill at all. A surge of anger rises in my heart, and I randomly throw her cheongsam and throw it at her face. She falls to the bed and starts to cry loudly.

Ascending Youzhou Terrace Poem: Chen Ziang

I see no ancient men before me,

Nor will I see those who come after.

Thinking of the boundlessness of heaven and earth,

I alone am saddened and weep!

Ancient Meaning: Li Qi

A man's duty is to serve on long campaigns,

From youth, a guest of You and Yan.

Betting on victory, beneath the horses' hooves,

He has always lightly valued his seven-foot frame.

Killing men, none dare step forward,

His beard is like thorny hedgehog bristles.

Yellow clouds beneath the Long Mountains, white clouds fly,

Not yet able to repay, thoughts cannot return.

The young woman of Liaodong, fifteen years old,

Is accustomed to playing the pipa, understands singing and dancing.

Now, from the Qiang flute, a cold sound issues,

Causing the tears of our army to fall like rain!

Qin Song: Li Qi

The host has wine to view this evening,

Please play the qin for the Guangling guest.

The moon shines on the city walls, birds fly halfway,

Frost chills ten thousand trees, wind enters clothing.

The copper furnace and bright candles add light,

First plays Green Water, then Chu Consort.

One sound already moves all creatures to silence,

The four seats are speechless, the stars almost fade.

I have been sent to Qing Huai for a thousand miles,

Dare I tell you that my journey from Yunshan begins here!

*Shen Bao* Local Supplement: Film Special - The Reason Why “New Type” People Have Difficulty Being Filmed 99

Combination of Special Features Creates the Chimera Face Type.

Illusions of Preconceived Notions Dominate Audience Preferences.

In a company, a meeting was convened. Seven or eight magnates gathered in a large conference hall. There, a long and wide conference table was situated, surrounded by high-backed chairs, and the floor was covered with a thick Beijing carpet. Everyone was smoking cigars, and when one person spoke, several others chatted amongst themselves in whispers. In this way, they handled several routine matters. Suddenly, a person stood up and proposed a motion. The motion was based on sound reasoning, repeatedly tested and proven, and unlikely to ever be overturned. However, that person did not need to make a solemn matter of it. Only when everyone's idle chatter had subsided and they were all ears, did he raise his voice to speak: "What our film industry urgently needs at the moment is new faces!" Sure enough, everyone sat up straight, and even stopped smoking their cigars, indicating their complete attention and agreement to this issue. Soon, they relaxed somewhat again, resuming their whispering and secret conversations. But the motion to seek out new types of people was eventually unanimously passed.

How to seek out new types of people then became the most important issue at hand. Of course, film industry magnates could not stand on the street and select new types of people from the passing pedestrians. However, they all felt that once something was worth wanting, it was worth seeking out with all their might. Thus, a detailed plan was drawn up. Many plans were made, and beauty contests were the most common and effective, because in addition to the positive effect of selecting the desired object, there were many side effects, such as the sensational publicity effect on society, etc. So they decided to adopt the beauty contest approach. The newspapers of major cities were invited to participate in the grand event together. Their news editors were, of course, happy to agree, because they knew that any news about the women's world would certainly cause a sensation in society.

Soon, a new list had been drawn up – Miss Kansas City, Miss Valley Forge, and so on. But this time, it was slightly different from all previous ones. In addition to the essential beauty, the qualifications of this group of ladies also included a special charm, which was the so-called new type of face. This group of beauties with new types of faces then gathered together in a warm place on one day. They were all dressed in exquisite and form-fitting bathing suits, each one elegant and charming, with a thousand kinds of grace and beauty. After exhibiting themselves to the public, they each received a train ticket to Hollywood and a contract from a film company, filled with ant-sized characters, all terms and conditions. They also had no time to read it in detail.

This group of beauties cheerfully traveled together to Hollywood. The film company magnates then subjected them to a detailed review one by one. Sure enough, this selection was uniquely insightful and extraordinary. Although one of them looked somewhat like Joan Crawford from afar, they thought that she would certainly be eliminated on her own in the future, so they did not take it to heart. But when the three-month trial period was over, nineteen of the twenty new beauties were useless and had to be sent home with one-way train tickets. Only the twentieth one, who usually looked somewhat like Joan Crawford, was simply indistinguishable from Joan in front of the camera. She was kept because she was photogenic. The others, compared to her, were more beautiful and had better figures, but they were all failures. Why? No one wanted to get to the bottom of it. Fortunately, it was clear that they were not popular, so what was the point of getting to the bottom of it?

According to Yuan, Chimera was a faithful reporter, but for some reason, Lidi's fair beauty was always considered more radiant than Aina's dark beauty when reprinted on film, even though Aina's true beauty was indeed far superior to Lidi's. Furthermore, the combination of several facial features is not necessarily called beauty, but it is very easy to be filmed. Large eyes, high cheekbones, a wide forehead, and a pointed chin, when combined, create a Chimera face. However, what has been said above is still just empty talk, difficult to define. What is most important, even more important than beauty, is an illusion, an illusion of exoticism, an illusion of health, an illusion of elegance, an illusion of mystery, and so on. So, Clara Bow had the illusion of "it" and she had the key to film fame and did not have to worry about not succeeding. Of course, illusion is also not something that can be grasped concretely. (To be continued)

Film Review: *Cleopatra*: Ji Han 100

*Cleopatra* – Da Guangming

Cecil B. DeMille! This master of the silver screen is truly too familiar to Chinese audiences. He expresses each of his plays with a heavy hand. In his films, there are grand scenes, large crowds, a heavy atmosphere, all of which demonstrate his magnificent power. These, from *The Sign of the Cross* to *Cleopatra*, all demonstrate his unique style.

People will not forget that Cecil B. DeMille is a religious filmmaker. At the same time, it can be said that he is a historical dramatist. From a religious point of view, a writer who serves religion is by no means an accidental attempt. Due to *The Ten Commandments*, *The King of Kings*, and *The Sign of the Cross*, etc., they all illustrate that he is a faithful preacher of Christianity. It is said that the Roman Pope once gave him a large amount of money as a reward, and he has a very honorable position in the Vatican. But from another perspective, the reason why he adopts religious themes is perhaps because he is very interested in tragic stories. This can be proved by his production of *The Godless Girl* or the historical drama *Cleopatra*, because there are no religious colors in them. In addition, there is also the slightly satirical *The Plainsman*, which is not for religious preaching, although the idea of imperialism in invading colonies is quite strong in the work.

It is very clear that none of Cecil B. DeMille's works does not express his old conceptual form. Today, he should be called a gentleman. As far as this work is concerned, the so-called historical narrative certainly has its effect on Cecil B. DeMille today. For example, Queen Cleopatra of Egypt wants to marry Caesar, the King of Rome. She hopes that Egypt and Rome can live in peace. The so-called idea that the King of Egypt should submit to Rome is ridiculed here. Furthermore, the significance of peace is expressed in General Antony, who breaks his spear to show his determination. But at the same time, it shows that the so-called military actions of radical elements attacking Egypt destroyed the so-called peace, and the Queen and Antony died for their country as a result.

In all aspects, this film is quite satisfactory to people, grand, sublime, and the enchanting charm of women. However, in terms of film art, the so-called change of style by the author, inserting modern dances into ancient history, will not but be criticized. However, it must be said that when people describe ancient history, it is like painting a ghost. Who can decide that the ghost is not painted realistically?

Review of (College Rhythm): You Jing 101

"College Rhythm" – Cathay Film Co.

(Sweet and gorgeous songs), (joyful and silly laughter), (beautiful and graceful women, romance), and everything else that can be used to embellish and provide forgetful enjoyment of this New Year of 1935, are fully applied, summoned, and enjoyed in this College Rhythm. Naturally, the whole world has spent 1934 in turmoil, thrills, worries, and madness. Although it is well known that everything that comes with this 1935 may be even more unpleasant, in these first few days, let's put aside everything and have a perverted amount of fun. Who can say anything? Therefore, films such as *Transatlantic Merry-Go-Round*, *The Merry Widow*, and this *College Rhythm* are used to embellish and respond to the times. Responding to the New Year holiday in this Eastern metropolis | Shanghai |.

As we follow the crowded group of nobles to watch this College Rhythm, we can't help but feel that what this film expresses, no matter how much sweet music, wild laughter, and sexual romance are used to cover up and intersperse, inevitably reveals the original face of this society. Such as football, and various other sports are also rigidified by this social system, and the original meaning of people going to exercise, the athletic performers are turned into commodities to make money for others, and due to economic panic, overproduction, followed by the poor living of the laboring masses, the consumer purchasing power is so low that it is impossible to be lower, the commercial depression formed in the so-called learned people, no matter how they use rationalized theories and methods to manage, to reform, they are also (business is greatly declining) and have to use (players with 85,000 fans) to call, in order to seek deformed (excellent results, business is booming) and other facts.

Speaking of the technical success of this film, there are naturally things that we cannot deny. From the casting of (the so-called scholars who work hard at books) and (the football players who have no real learning) to the attitudes of the two rival shop owners, they have all properly achieved a successful situation. In the noisy scenes of the football field, banquet party, and the opening of the department store, the application of air control and sound effects is excellent. However, the emphasis on the cheerleader's performance and many dance numbers in the store are exaggerated too much, forming a disproportion in the overall amount of the film. For the sake of excitement, they do not hesitate to over-emphasize certain scenes, which is a common problem with many Hollywood films without content. Therefore, the so-called excitement in College Rhythm is just excitement.

The actors have done as much as they should in such a script. Among them, Lanny Ross's performance of Riley is more profound. The so-called Miss Shanghai, Lyda Roberti, appears here as a clown, and there is not much to admire.

United Artists' new film, *Transatlantic Merry-Go-Round*, is Sweet Sister Neisse Carle's most successful work. Not only is the song and dance novel, but the plot is even better. All countries consider it a spectacle of song and dance films this year.

Measures to Protect Local Sugar in Guangdong Province 103

|Changes to Inspection Areas by the National Products Office|

Correspondent from Shantou reports: Since the National Products Promotion Office established by the provincial government implemented new measures to protect locally produced sugar, rural sugar producers have been subjected to various forms of oppression. The Chaozhou Fellow Townsmen Association in Shanghai, the Shantou Sugar Industry Association, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Puning Fellow Townsmen Association in Shantou, and the Chaoyang Fellow Townsmen Association in Shantou have all recognized the difficulty in implementing these new measures and have successively telegraphed the Department of Construction to strongly advocate for their revision. The Department of Construction then ordered the National Products Office in Shantou to investigate and respond. The Shantou National Products Office considered the measures absolutely necessary; therefore, the Department of Construction refused to revoke its decision. Consequently, the National Products Office issued a revised announcement regarding the protection of local sugar, stating: (To prevent the smuggling of protected local sugar, it is necessary to inspect all sugar slabs and sugar pieces transported for sale from various districts to determine their authenticity and prevent adulteration with foreign sugar. However, many farmers and merchants in various districts do not understand this intention. Any inspection leads to suspicion and concern, causing unnecessary alarm among local sugar merchants, which is regrettable. Therefore, we are making slight adjustments to the inspection methods. Local sugar from areas far from the sea with less smuggling, such as the upper reaches of the Northwest River and districts north of the East River,

upon arrival in this city, will be exempt from inspection. For sugar products from coastal areas, such as Dongguan, Sanshui, Gaoyao, the Five Districts [Xinhui, Taishan, Kaiping, Enping, Heshan], Liangyang, Nan[hai], Fan[yu], Zhong[shan], Shun[de], Chao[zhou], Pu[ning], Hui[yang], Rao[ping], Haifeng, Lufeng, and districts near Hong Kong and Macau, samples must be taken according to regulations and sent to the Guangzhou First District Sugar Manufacturing Plant for chemical analysis to determine their authenticity.) Furthermore, the Guangdong sugar industry has been impacted by the government's strict control measures. A significant amount of local sugar in Guangzhou has been detained. Among those already analyzed and penalized, on December 12th, Qingyuan Wu Xinghao's 1,352 catties were found to be half adulterated with foreign sugar, resulting in confiscation and a fine of 42 yuan, 8 jiao, and 1 cent. Xiang Xinghao, transported by the Benyuan Company from Haikou, had 1,457 catties, also found to be half adulterated with foreign sugar, receiving the same penalty as above. Heng Dehao from Hanguangxu in Yingde, weighing 1,840 catties, was found to be entirely foreign sugar upon analysis. As it had already been sold, a sugar price of 118 yuan and 4 hao was to be paid. Wan Yuantaihao, transported from Dianbai, had 800 catties, found to be mostly adulterated with foreign sugar, and was fined two-thirds of the sugar price, totaling 58 yuan, 6 hao, and 7 cents. Additionally, Shui Dong Tailaihao transported 450 catties, and since the sugar had already been sold, a price of 49 yuan and 5 hao was to be paid. Many other firms have also had their goods seized. Sugar merchants, dissatisfied, jointly requested the Department of Construction to abolish the factory exit law, stating that all sugar slabs transported from various districts are made from sugarcane juice from the fields. They are now being fined or having their goods confiscated entirely. Without prior clear announcements from the Department regarding distinguishing samples of foreign sugar, local sugar, and mixtures of foreign sugar, the current analysis is neither transparent nor accurate. The results of the analysis of the penalized local sugar are based on approximate judgments, which is unfair and difficult to accept. However, with the precedent for fines established, and local sugar increasingly restricted, the government-operated national sugar should be able to expand its sales.

Introduction of Yellow River Water into Huiji in Henan Province 104

River Dredging Completed

Project Nearing Completion

Correspondent from Kaifeng reports: The project to divert Yellow River water into the Huiji River, organized by the Department of Construction, has been underway for over three years since dredging the Huiji River began at the end of the twentieth year. The project is now nearing completion. A summary is provided below. The Huiji River originates from the nursery of the Department of Construction in the southeastern corner of Kaifeng city and ends in Tuocheng, passing through Chenliu, Qixian, and Suixian, covering a total distance of 137 kilometers. The dredging project was initiated in December of the twentieth year and completed in August of the twenty-second year, involving the excavation of 4,964,600 cubic meters of earth, the construction of six new bridges, the renovation of five bridges, and the construction of 130 culverts. However, the soil on both banks of the river is mostly sandy and requires irrigation to produce abundant crops. Due to insufficient water in the Huiji River, a plan was formulated to supplement the water source after dredging to facilitate irrigation for the farmland on both banks. A new river was opened from the Erdao Dike in Kaifeng, passing through Beishan Village, Nanshan Village, crossing the city wall, passing through Zhongguanzhuang and Sun Li Tangzhuang, to the western gate of Kaifeng, and then turning southeast to the nursery of the Department of Construction in the southeastern corner of the city, reaching the Huiji River. It is 13,300 meters long and named the Huanghui River. Sluice gates were installed at the Erdao Dike river mouth and where it crosses the city wall for control. The above excavation and sluice gate projects have long been completed. Furthermore, a canal was opened from each of Liuyuankou and Heigangkou, connecting to the water pools of the dikes at these two locations and joining the Huanghui River at the Erdao Dike river mouth, named the Liuyuankou Water Diversion Canal and the Heigangkou Water Diversion Canal respectively, to divert accumulated water from the water pools inside the dikes at these two locations to the Huanghui River and supplement the Huiji River's source. A sluice gate was also trial-installed where the Heigangkou Water Diversion Canal crosses the dike to prevent accidents. Additionally, two sets of siphon pipes were installed on the Liuyuankou Dike, and six sets of siphon pipes were installed on the Heigangkou Dike to draw water from the Yellow River into the water pools. After clarification, the water flows through the diversion canals into the Huanghui River to supplement the water source. The siphon pipes have an inner diameter of 6 inches and a length of about 160 meters each. The eight sets have been fully installed, with a total outflow of over 6 cubic meters per second. The Liuyuankou siphon pipes are now fully installed, and the Heigangkou siphon pipes are about to be installed. Both water diversion canals have started construction and can be fully completed within a month. However, the area of farmland along the Huiji River awaiting irrigation is vast, and the amount of water diverted by these siphon pipes is minimal, requiring further expansion to meet the needs. Moreover, the water within the city of Kaifeng stagnates, and the soil along the lakes and rivers is highly saline. To remove pollutants and improve the soil quality, the Department of Construction specially opened a branch canal on the eastern bank of the Huanghui River at Sun Li Tangzhuang, diverting water through the northwestern corner of the city. A water gate was built where it passes through the city, equipped with new-style gates for opening and closing, named the Libian Gate. Water flows eastward from the Libian Gate into the Pan Yang Lake, dividing into two branches. One branch follows the city southward, then turns eastward at the southwestern corner of the city, heading straight to the Shuimen Gate in the eastern part of the city. This Shuimen Gate has also been renovated and equipped with new-style gates, named the Jiliang Gate. The other branch passes through Pan Yang Lake, follows the city eastward to near the Kaifeng Meteorological Station, then turns southward, merging with the other branch before the Shuimen Gate. After the two branches merge, they pass through the Shuimen Gate and flow into the Huiji River. Currently, all sections of the river channels are unobstructed. After the channels were opened, bridges were built over the rivers and canals for transportation convenience, including three bridges over the Yuankou Water Diversion Canal, five bridges over the Heigangkou Water Diversion Canal, four bridges over the Huanghui River, four bridges over the section of the river from Sun Li Tangzhuang to the Libian Gate, and 24 bridges over the Huiji River within the city. These bridges are either completed or under construction and will soon be fully completed. To facilitate drainage on both banks of the river, over a hundred culverts are being gradually constructed and will be completed soon. From now on, the cityscape of Kaifeng can be improved, and the farmland along the Huiji River will no longer have to worry about drought. (December 30th)

Chief of the Provincial Security Department Visits Songjiang 105

Mr. Xiang Zhizhuang, the Chief of the Provincial Security Department and Standing Committee Member of the Provincial Anti-Opium Association, arrived in Songjiang at 4 PM on the third. Robbery in Xiahengjing, Tinglin 106

The home of Li Zhiqin, a resident of the 17th district of Xiahengjing in Tinglin, was suddenly raided by over ten robbers speaking the local dialect at about 1 AM on the first night. They entered the house with hemp ropes and other items to search and rob, taking over two hundred yuan in silver, seventeen beads, over fifty pieces of clothing, two leather garments, and sixty bolts of cloth before escaping with the loot.

News of Court President's Transfer 107

Wang Sixian, the President of the County Court in this county, has served for over two years, handling cases fairly and earning praise from his superiors. It is now learned that Mr. Wang has been ordered to be transferred to the Nantong Court. It is rumored that a Mr. Zhou will succeed him, and the handover will be completed soon.

Suzhou

Dismissal of Patrol Officer for Protecting Opium Case 108

The Provincial Anti-Opium Association previously sent personnel to Suzhou, where they uncovered a large-scale opium den at No. 17 Yong'an Lane outside Xumen. Over ten opium offenders were arrested on the spot. Patrol Officer Fang Ying of the First Precinct of the Third Bureau was suspected of protecting the den. The Provincial Anti-Opium Association reported this to the provincial government, which in turn instructed the Department of Civil Affairs to dismiss Fang Ying. Xu Shulian, the Chief of the Third Bureau, was also deemed culpable. The county was ordered yesterday to investigate and handle the matter.

Bill Collector Robbed En Route 109

The Shanghai Yuan Yuan Farm has a branch company in Dingjia Lane outside Xumen in Suzhou. Due to having over forty client households in Wujiang, they specifically sent employee Yin Ronghai on the second to collect payments. He was returning to Suzhou via the Sujia Road in a rented car when, upon reaching the first bridge north of Jiapu Bridge (i.e., the fifth bridge south of Baodai Bridge), he saw six people on the bridge who ordered him to stop, claiming they wanted to buy the Wuxian Daily. Yin replied that he was not a newspaper vendor. The six people immediately rushed forward, pushed the car off the road, and dragged Yin into a small boat. They robbed him of all the collected payments, totaling forty-four yuan and eight jiao, a robe, and a pair of cotton pants. They bound his hands, rowed two or three li to a desolate spot, threw Yin onto the riverbank, and then sailed back into Taihu Lake in the same boat. Yin later escaped back to where he had been robbed, where he found the car still there, but it had been vandalized with knives.

Wuxi

Robbery Occurs Amidst New Year's Celebrations 110

The resident Shen Rengui of Liu Chuanqiao in Houshan Township, Sixth District, had a modest fortune. Suddenly, around midnight the day before yesterday, over ten burly robbers broke into his house, arbitrarily searching and robbing. Shen's wife, hearing the noise, came out and was immediately bound and forbidden from making any noise. After about half an hour, the robbers left with their loot. Upon inspection, the total loss was over one hundred yuan.

Ten Years Imprisonment for Selling Poison Pills 111

On July 26th of last year, the Inspection Office of the Municipal Public Security Bureau apprehended three individuals, Zhang Wu, Zhang Miao, and Lu Afu, for selling poison pills at No. 22 Heng Street in Ximen. They also seized two hundred gray poison pills and thirty red poison pills. They were escorted to the county government and then transferred to the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters. After a thorough interrogation by military judge Zou Dian, Zhang Wu was found guilty of violating Article 3 of the Provisional Regulations for Strict Prohibition of Potent Narcotics and sentenced to life imprisonment. Considering the woman's ignorance and the fact that her husband, Zhang Aquan (who is still at large), was the principal offender, and in accordance with Article 14 of the same regulations, Article 77 and Article 80, Section 2 of the Criminal Law were applied, reducing the sentence by half to ten years of imprisonment. Zhang Miao's suspicion of aiding and abetting was insufficient, and a verdict of innocence was pronounced in accordance with Article 316 of the Criminal Procedure Law. Lu Afu was using poison pills and, in accordance with Article 5 of the above regulations, was returned to the original county to be sent to a hospital for mandatory rehabilitation. The decision was approved by the Nanchang Headquarters and sent back to the county government yesterday for execution.

Changzhou

Arrest of Robbers in Robbery Case Near Dingyan 112

The home of farmer Zhang Yaoxian near Dingyan Town outside the East Gate of Wuyi County was robbed late on December 31st of last year. The victim was stabbed and injured. On the second of this month, the Fourth Police Station of the First Public Security Bureau outside the East Gate, together with detectives from the First Bureau, apprehended three robbers, Zhou Fuqing, Yu Mingluo, and Chen Baoming, and six suspects, including Yu Fengwu, at the Xiaguan Hall east of Baijia Bridge. Changshu

Release of Former Security Team Leader in Lost Gun Case 113

The former Second Company Commander of the Security Team, Liao Zhiyuan, was dismissed from his position, and the vacancy was filled by Yu Quangui, appointed by the provincial committee. During the handover, it was suddenly discovered that a box cannon had been lost. According to the statement of Secretary Yao Zhengjia, it had been borrowed by the former Security Team Leader, Fan Zhengshan, and subsequently sold. The team considered the matter significant and detained former Team Leader Fan for interrogation. Fan consistently denied the accusation. The team then submitted a request to the province for instructions. Subsequently, Fan's wife, Ms. Yu Jianru, appealed to the province for assistance. As Fan had been appointed to a position in the Qingpu County Security Team, the Provincial Security Department investigated and determined that he had been falsely accused. The province ordered the county to release him. Now that the county has received the order, Fan has been released. Secretary Yao is responsible for compensating for the lost firearm. Fan is scheduled to take office in Qingpu on the fifth.

Closing Ceremony of the National Products Exhibition 114

Over forty national product factories in Shanghai organized a mobile exhibition to promote national products and display them in various inland areas. The exhibition arrived in Changshu at the beginning of last month and set up stalls in the area of the old Chenghuang Temple. The opening ceremony took place on the tenth.

Unfortunately, since the opening, the weather has been unfavorable, with continuous rain for nearly half a month, resulting in poor business. From the opening until now, the total turnover has been only over twelve thousand yuan. Due to high expenses, it has been decided to close on the fifth and move the exhibition to Yixing. Some manufacturers had already closed their stalls and left on the third.

Haimen

Provincial Order to Crack Down on Ferry Boat Extortion 115

Ships operating on the Shanghai route, due to the lack of docks in various ports of this county, require ferry boats to transport passengers and cargo. The fares for these ferry boats have never been clearly regulated, leading to arbitrary extortion by boat operators, causing hardship for travelers. County residents Pan Huanwen, Lu Boheng, and others submitted a petition to the provincial government to strictly crack down on this practice. Yesterday (the 29th), the provincial government ordered the county government to investigate and stop this practice promptly and to draft reasonable fare rates for the ferry routes in each port, taking into account the distance, and submit them for approval.
